### SantiMod
4/25/2021, 2:33:53 PM

REBIRTH: GENESIS OF A METAVERSE UPDATE:

1. We are aware of several issues purchasers are experiencing with the claiming/redemption process within the Star Atlas Dashboard. Please do not worry. All of these transactions were processed entirely on chain. They are all publicly accessible. We are working on resolving the UI issue, but your assets are NOT at risk. If you have purchased a poster and recieved a 'confirmation' notice, YOU WILL SEE THE POSTER IN YOUR INVENTORY SOON. The team is working through the weekend to reconcile any non-updated balances.

2. There are a number of questions we have received regarding the specific mechanics of the poster series. @SW4GN3R will be recording a video later today with answers to many of those questions.

Mentions: @SW4GN3R

### SantiMod
5/1/2021, 2:09:59 PM

I will once again paste this:

THE NETWORK IS CURRENTLY EXPERIENCING SOME CONGESTION CAUSING LOSS OF FUNCTIONALITY ACROSS A VARIETY OF APPLICATIONS, INCLUDING THE STAR ATLAS MARKETPLACE. ALL OF THE BEST MINDS IN THE SPACE ARE WORKING TOWARDS RESOLVING THIS. DESPITE THE INCONVENIENCE, IT MEANS THE NETWORK IS GROWING CONSIDERABLY AND CREATING THE NEED FOR NEW SOLUTIONS. THIS IS A POSITIVE. CHECK BACK THROUGHOUT THE DAY, AS OUR TEAM IS ALSO WORKING ON ALTERNATIVE ENDPOINT SOLUTIONS.

### SantiMod
5/1/2021, 5:24:32 PM

We're extending the sale of Poster 1 (Discover of Iris) for 24h due to recent instability with the Solana & Serum RPC endpoints. This is to give everyone a fair chance to buy the poster.

---

### SantiMod
5/1/2021, 5:39:14 PM

We aren't letting 'everyone' buy. We are letting the final few who were trying to purchase today but were not able to due to network instability. As I said earlier, while we want to be conscientious of those who purchased earlier in the week, we also want to be fair to those who were unable to purchase resulting from this instability. As a result, we have extended Poster 1 for 24 hours and are seeking to implmement some immediate alternative fixes to the RPC infrastructure so we do not encounter these problems going forward.

If anyone would like to SELL one of their posters on the open Serum DEX, this is the marketplace for DOI: If anyone would like to place a SELL order on their DOI, it can be done so through this link: https://dex.projectserum.com/#/market/AYXTVttPfhYmn3jryX5XbRjwPK2m9445mbN2iLyRD6nq

1. Click '+' to add a market on the top left of dex.projectserum.com
2. Add AYXTVttPfhYmn3jryX5XbRjwPK2m9445mbN2iLyRD6nq
3. You can define Marketplace ID, and base pair ticker is DOI
4. You have to manually add the market, so the link provided will not load by default

We are rectifying the situation of the Neil Armstrong poster rewards to be consistent with the feedback that we’ve received from you, our community. 

The new poster will not contain the same exact rewards that can be obtained by DOI, nor will it count for achieving Tiers in ReBirth. 

These are the updated rewards that you will obtain by purchasing Neil Armstrong’s poster: 

Ship Rewards
1x Opal Jet
1x Exclusive White Hot Skin for Opal Jet 

Mining Claims Starter Package
1x Claim Stake - Tier 1
1x Mining Station Power Plant - Tier 1
1x Mining Drill - Tier 1
1x Orbital Space Station with Trading Deck - Tier 1 

Access Rewards
1x Faction Passport
1x Legends Badge 

Legends Rewards
1x Neil Armstrong Uniform Patch
1x Vintage Astronaut Suit
1x Vintage Orbiting Satellite

 Any poster/asset that is in either an OPEN order, UNCLAIMED, or UNSETTLED status on the dex/inventory will NOT be counted in the snapshot.

### SantiMod
9/1/2021, 5:26:30 PM

Community Announcement!

 As we know how much you’re supporting Star Atlas, we want to give something back to you, that’s why we created the Star Atlas Diplomacy Alliance Program!

 This Program has the objective to reward you for inviting your friends to the Star Atlas Discord Server! 

 How does it work?
The Alliance consists of a ticket bonus structure where we run monthly NFT & token drawings. The more you refer, the more you earn!

 How can you earn tickets?
- You’ll earn one ticket for every friend that joins the server using your invite
- There will be bounties and competitions for extra tickets (Meme competitions, emoji creations, etc) 
- Bonus tickets when you reach 3, 6 and 10 joins from your invites!

(There's a cap of 10 joins per user)

 What are the prizes for this month?
Grand Prize: Opal Jetjet 
First Prize: $100 usd worth of ATLAS
Second Prize: Opal Jet

Winners will be picked using a lottery system, the more tickets you own, the more chances you have!

### SantiMod
9/29/2021, 8:16:30 AM

Only one day left for the Star Atlas Diplomacy Alliance draw to take place!!

 How does it work?
The Alliance consists of a ticket bonus structure where we run monthly NFT & token drawings. The more you refer, the more you earn!

 How can you earn tickets?
- You’ll earn one ticket for every friend that joins the server using your invite
- There will be bounties and competitions for extra tickets (Meme competitions, emoji creations, etc) 
- Bonus tickets when you reach 3, 6 and 10 joins from your invites!

(There's a cap of 10 joins per user)

 What are the prizes for this month?
Grand Prize: Opal Jetjet 
First Prize: $100 usd worth of ATLAS
Second Prize: Opal Jet

Winners will be picked using a lottery system, the more tickets you own, the more chances you have!

### SantiMod
11/10/2021, 3:21:35 PM

Pearce C9 Update  

Our team encountered a data validation bug that prevented 17 Pearce C9 ships from getting minted, and another 35 from being listed.

Directly upon the bug being hotfixed, an additional 52 ships were listed, with 17 added to the USDC pair, and 35 to the ATLAS pair. They all went out at Wave 3 price as planned.

Thanks for your support and understanding!

### SantiMod
1/17/2022, 7:40:42 AM
_Edited_

The much requested ⁠unknown channel has been created and is ready to be used!  

In this channel guilds will have a space to post recruitment messages, updates and events!  

Please read the rules before posting anything!  


Rules
 
- Only one post per 24 hours, per guild. Guild leaders: please coordinate this with your members so we don't experience unnecessary guild spam. A guild that constantly spams will be frowned upon by the members of the community.- Post only about guild events, guild updates or for recruitment purposes.
- No chatting, not even guild-related. This includes replying to guild-messages. Please use ⁠unknown
This channel is set to allow only 1 message per person per 24 hours . Or in other words: After posting a message, you will be unable to do so again for the next 24 hours afterwards. 
However: No guild is allowed to post more than a single message per 24 hours. Again, guild leaders please coordinate this with your members so moderation is easier. 
 
Moderation
 
- The moderation team will remove chatter. 
- The moderation team will remove multiple messages of the same guild within the 24h timeframe. Please coordinate internally and follow the Netiquette (Rules). 
- We are all aware that mistakes happen, please do not make mistakes happen consistently 
- If you feel your message was moderated wrongfully, please reach out to one of our @Mod via DM

Only @Mod will moderate this channel. @Community Moderator are not able to moderate here, to prevent any accusation of biased moderation

Global Polishing Update: 

Hey guys!

Furthering our overall user experience, we wanted to inform our community of some minor changes that will be carried out in the near future.

Before you connect your wallet, you will need to confirm:  (1) That you agree to our Terms of Service (https://staratlas.com/terms-of-service) and (2) that you have read our Privacy Policy (https://staratlas.com/privacy-policy). 

Both documents have been on our sites for a while, and we want to make sure that everyone in the community is aware of their content and our policies.

In addition, we are also implementing features to ensure you can disable cookies to protect your privacy if you so desire. We are just giving you guys a heads up before implementing this so you are not caught off-guard by the new design with the upcoming changes to our website.  Should you have any questions about this update, please do not hesitate to reach out to us!

### SantiMod
4/13/2022, 9:28:47 AM

Technical community update: 

This message addresses the situation with failing blockchain transactions for Toolkit purchases in the Galactic Marketplace at Play.staratlas.com that many community members are experiencing while playing SCORE.

Working with engineers at Solana, we have determined that the reason for transaction failures are difficulties in the wider blockchain network itself. 

More specifically, hundreds of thousands of largely duplicate transactions per second that are being sent across the network for validation by bots, causing congestion. This causes some transactions over a certain limit of data size or requiring time-sensitive information to fail, and one such transaction is the Toolkit one. 

We are working on solving the issue in two ways: 

 We are in the process of implementing an informational banner in our Marketplace that will show users a real-time health and status of the Solana network and enable our community to receive instant feedback on the likelihood of success of their transactions.

 We are also in touch with the Solana network, which is working on important blockchain upgrades, the first one being rolled out in early May and aiming to bring a long-term solution to chain congestion.

Thank you for your continued patience and support in resolving the issue. We will keep you updated as the situation evolves.

Power to the people!

### SantiMod
5/1/2022, 1:21:24 PM

@here  Community Update  

If you're resupplying your fleet this Sunday, you're seeing $ATLAS rewards calculation as slightly out of sync with consumption of 4R resources.

Please know that ATLAS rewards & R4 burn is still being calculated correctly on #Solana's back end.

The discrepancy is due to the user interface clock being temporarily out of sync after the Solana network restart last night.

The #Solana Team has confirmed that this issue will disappear once block times across the network resyncronize. 

Thank you for your patience!

### DominicVainMod
7/31/2022, 5:17:32 PM

@here 


 Community Update: Star Atlas DAO Team Locking 

As Star Atlas DAO rewards for locking your tokens for PVP (POLIS Voting Power) go live on August 2, 2022, we want to remain open and transparent about our intentions with the ATMTA team's tokens, and how we're taking a community-first approach.

In short, we will be locking the minimum amount of tokens necessary to ensure ATMTA has enough PVP during the early development of the ecosystem--in the near term, approximately 65% of total PVP. This also ensures that the community gets ultimate control of the DAO over the longer term. We will be managing the team's PVP dynamically, with an emphasis on long duration locks. Our initial team lock has a duration of 5 years. We believe our approach is unprecedented for a blockchain-based project of this complexity and scope, and is the best way for us to demonstrate our commitment to deliver on the groundbreaking vision that is Star Atlas.

Team Locking Principles in More Detail:
- We will be dynamically managing the ATMTA locked tokens to maintain a PVP target weight in the Star Atlas DAO at a ~65% total weight, or enough to provide a buffer against new daily locks, and assuming the actual day-to-day percentage will vary.
- Although the Economics Paper makes clear the team's balance of 108mm POLIS is available for locking, we will not lock the full balance at the outset in order to ensure maximum community benefit and that ATMTA does not collect an overwhelming share of emissions.
- Over time, we intend to lock the entire Team balance as additional POLIS enter the locker, and we will be locking tokens across the 5-year as well as the 4- and 3-year locking period.

### SantiMod
8/2/2022, 7:29:52 PM
_Edited_

@everyone There are rumors of a large scale exploit in the Solana blockchain. This is what you can do to stay safe:

1. Go to Settings on your Phantom wallet
2. Trusted Apps
3. Revoke Permissions for all the apps

You can also move your funds to a cold wallet like Ledger if you have access to one. 

Please stay safe!

### SantiMod
8/16/2022, 12:13:29 PM

SHORT VIDEO CONTEST UPDATE 

Good news! 
Prize update: Winner will now receive 3 Fimbul Lowbies (!!) and eternal glory for your faction!

Videos are now due by 11:59PM UTC on Tuesday Aug. 23 (extra time!)

Winner will be announced during the Aug. 26 Town Hall.

How to enter:
- Make a video from the viewpoint of yourself or a @StarAtlas character 
- Don’t worry about budget or reaching AAA quality
- Keep it short (ideally under 4 min., 8 min. max)
- Keep it clean/family friendly
- Submit via Twitter 
- Tag @WeAreStarAtlas & #StarAtlasSummer 
No purchase necessary

There will be three “anonymous” judges:
- A voice of the people (rhymes with “MAHN-tee”)
- A Star Atlas team member 
- Hollywood producer/screenwriter Gavin Harris (Co-Executive Producer, Chicago P.D. [NBC, 2021-22]; Co-Executive Producer, Law & Order - Special Victims Unit; Co-Executive Producer, CSI: Scene Investigation)

Judging criteria:
- Entertainment value
- Creativity

 Watch this video for inspiration: https://twitter.com/Boerged/status/1558130634996023297

Submissions are subject to the Star Atlas Terms of Service: https://staratlas.com/terms-of-service

### SantiMod
8/23/2022, 8:58:59 PM

Some of you may have noticed that Sollet is no longer on play.staratlas.com and govern.staratlas.com and we want to give some context so everyone knows what is going on.

Sollet support was removed by the developer and will be permanently removed as an option on the above 2 sites. We suggest using one of the "recommended" wallets instead. If you're affected by this change, we'll have a quick guide to migrate to Phantom from Sollet.

1. Install Phantom
2. Export Secret Recovery Phrase from Sollet
3. Import Secret Recovery Phrase to Phantom.

https://help.phantom.app/hc/en-us/articles/4406527601811-How-to-migrate-from-Sollet

Showroom will be live TODAY on the EPIC GAMES STORE! 

This is closed pre-alpha access and to gain access, you'll need a key.

https://store.epicgames.com/en-US/p/star-atlas-bead34

How keys are distributed:
Keys are distributed based on what Faction Fleet badge you have. The higher the badge, the more keys you receive. If you've enrolled your ships in faction fleet for at least 7 days and have the Seasoned Fleet badge, you'll be receiving a key.

The pre-alpha game keys for the Star Atlas Showroom can be found on the Profile page that can be accessed by clicking above "wallet connected" in play.staratlas.com. Once you are in the profile page, you will see a "claim game keys" button at the top right of the screen.

Below, you'll find a graphic displaying the details on how many keys each Faction Fleet badge tier receives.

If you need help redeeming your key, please head over to ⁠No Access  for a list of frequently asked questions.

### DominicVainMod
10/31/2022, 4:03:40 PM

@everyone 

   The Atlas Brew Revamp    

We'll be switching the way we do "Atlas Brews" in the future to help the community have a better audience experience. 

Before going into details, let me explain what The Atlas Brew is, for those of you who don't know. The Atlas Brew is a weekly community gathering, held on Wednesdays, where we discuss pre-determined topics, open-mic style, and have fun!

The Atlas Brew has turned into a sacred tradition in the Star Atlas community and it deserves more love. Going forward, The Atlas Brew will have 4 main topics that will be covered every month. 

New Schedule:  

First Wednesday of the Month - Theory Crafting Economics  
Second Wednesday of the Month - Theory Crafting Politics  
Third Wednesday of the Month - Theory Crafting Game Structure  
Fourth Wednesday of the Month - Freestyle and Community Updates  

These 4 main topics will happens every month with different sub topics every month. 

November Schedule:  

This new format will start in November, which means it's time to announce our schedule this month!

11/2 - Economics Topic (Bots, are they Good or Bad?)
11/9 - Politics Topic (Inner Faction Conflicts)
11/16 - Game Structure Topic (Use Cases for Resources)
11/23 - Freestyle and Community Updates
11/30 - Special Brew

The events are live now at the top left of the server, if you'd like to hit the "interested" button to be notified when we're live!

### DominicVainMod
11/2/2022, 2:05:52 PM

@everyone

Introducing Faction Trivia!    

Faction Trivia will be a Three Week event held on 11/11, 11/18 and 11/25 where the community can come and compete in a trivia event for their faction!

Only one faction can win. Will it be ONI, Ustur or MUD? 

Details:  
This event will be held in our #Voice Chat at 1 PM EST on 11/11, 11/18 and 11/25

Trivia questions will be asked and the first faction member to answer correctly gains a point for their faction. At the end of the three week event, the faction with the most points wins!

Prizing:  
Throughout this event, you'll gain 1 raffle ticket for each question you answer first and correctly for your faction. At the end, the winning faction's raffle tickets will double, which of course means the winning faction will have more chances to win prizes.

On top of that, the top scorer of the winning faction will also win a behind the scenes look at the Star Atlas team server. 

See you on 11/11 to start things off! 

https://discord.com/events/789226204980707409/1037441970466992178

@everyone 

Golden Era Start Sequence - Our Path Towards Tomorrow

Below, you'll find our new plan towards forging our path towards tomorrow and the future of Star Atlas. 

Titan Ship Sales
A mint of three titan ships, The Pearce T1, Busan — The Last Stand mk. VIII, and the Fimbul ECOS Superphoenix, under a limited-time decreasing discount program, which will also award unique commemorative skins to buyers.

Special Ship Sales
A unique selection of ships that will be sold under a limited-time decreasing discount program, which will also award unique commemorative skins to buyers. Current holders of those assets, as of the time of this release, will receive another ship as an airdrop.

Claim Stake Sales
All the necessary assets (claim stakes, mining drills, power plants, and others) for the mining operations of SAGE after the main net launch.

Central Space Station Cosmetic Land and Habitations Sale
The sale of claims to a portion of residential areas plots inside the Central Space Stations. Players who acquire these lands will be entitled to a variety of benefits listed later in this article.

If you'd like more details, an update on external funding initiatives, as well as some other juicy bonuses: https://medium.com/star-atlas/star-atlas-golden-era-start-sequence-our-path-towards-tomorrow-cb7d51f19c84

### DominicVainMod
11/21/2022, 11:08:36 PM

@everyone

Titan Ship Sales and Select Ship Discounts Will Go Live on Wednesday!


  Titan Ship Sales: 

The most accurate description of the dreadful power of a titan ship came from the Ustur General Pac.Eldr, during the convergence war, who said the following:

“The Titan needed to not waste a single round of ammo. As soon as its shadow covered the entire horizon of the world, our fleet was destroyed. If not physically, in every other possible manner.”

Now, three of those monsters will awake from their slumber, and the time and stage into which the competition for the galaxy's ultimate machines of war is already set.

The 3 Titans being sold are:
• 1x Pearce T1
• 1x Busan-The Last Stand mk. VIII
• 1x Fimbul ECOS Superphoenix (ECOS)

These Titans will be 80% off on release and will lose 10% of that discount every week, for 4 weeks. Also, each one of the acquired titans will entitle the buyer to a unique commemorative ship skin, representing participation in this historic event.


   Select Ship Discounts: 

In order to fight the aggressive expansion of outlaws in the Medium-Risk Zone, the Council of Peace is also promoting a special sale of the assets they seized from the Factions after the Convergence War.

Now, those ships will fly, not to wage war but to protect the peace.

The 6 ships being discounted are:
• Pearce D9
• Ogrika Sunpaa
• Busan Maiden Heart
• Fimbul Mamba
• Pearce R6
• Fimbul BYOS Tankship

These ships will be 80% off on release and will lose 10% of that discount every week, for 4 weeks. Discounted ships that are purchased will come with a custom skin airdrop.

To do justice to the members of our community who have acquired these ships at original price, we will be airdropping one bonus ship of the same kind per ship purchased based on a snapshot taken last week. 

Titan ship sales and select ship discounts will go live on 

 | Learn more: https://medium.com/star-atlas/flight-of-the-titans-manifesto-golden-era-f47b287e20d2

### DominicVainMod
11/29/2022, 2:03:14 PM

@everyone

The Path Towards Tomorrow: Phase 2 - CSS Land Plot and Claim Stake Sales

It's finally time to talk about and announce our date for Land and Claim Stakes!

 Land Plots on CSSs:

As most of you know, Central Space Stations are the heart of each faction, being in the most protected place in the galaxy, the Low Risk Zone. Players who acquire property on these stations will be able to live inside these seats of power and become part of an exclusive community.

• The sale of land plots will correspond to 10% of the total residential area of each Faction CSS, divided into 6 tiers.
• Brings utility as soon as the SAGE game is released, enabling our players to store and craft resources with benefits depending on the different tier of plot acquired.
• By acquiring land plots at this event, you will be entitled to be part of a VIP priority-access listing on the sale of commercial land at the station in the future. This will be restricted, of course, to commercial land of the same tier as the one you acquire in the coming sale.
• Buyers will receive a group of ships befitting their plot selection as well as receive a commemorative cosmetic NFT, memorializing participation in this historic event.

  Claim Stakes:

Claim Stakes are physical objects that must be transported to a chosen planet in order to lay claim to a plot on its surface. Claiming a planetary plot grants you, the owner, access to extracting available local resources, being the first step in the mining industry gameplay loop.

• All of the claim stakes below will be activated in the first mainnet release of SAGE to enable mining, crafting and starbase building.
• Immediate utility includes, In Faction Fleet (SCORE), these claim stakes will be able to supply up to a certain ship size, depending on what tier you own. For example, to power an XS ship, you'll need a Tier 1 claim. These power rates increase all the way up to a Legendary Tier 5 claim stake which will generate enough power in SCORE to power a Capital sized ship. (This point only applies to Faction Fleet, SAGE will have different utility)

These sales will start on 

  | Details on pricing and tiers: https://staratlasgame.medium.com/the-path-towards-tomorrow-phase-2-css-land-plot-and-claim-stake-sales-3e5ca3d15c5c

@everyone Joni Awards!

Introducing the first annual Joni Awards! 

The Joni Awards is a new annual event in which we celebrate our community, the members and contributions they did and continue doing to make this the best community in the world. From the bottom of our heart, thank you. We couldn't have made it this far without every single one of you. 

These are 100% community-decided awards. In case of evidence of tempering with the votes in individual award categories, the Star Atlas team reserves the right to examine and modify the pool of votes to achieve a fair result

 Nominations:

From now until December 5, nominate your favorite community members, guilds and projects for a variety of different award categories:

• Community Member of the Year
• Most Knowledgeable Star Atlas Community Member
• Community Helper of the Year
• Community-Created Project of the Year
• Meme of the Year
• Small Guild of the Year
• Medium Guild of the Year
• Large Guild of the Year
• Best Guild Website
• Star Atlas Video of the Year by a Content Creator
• Content Creator of the Year
• Favorite Solana Project

 Final Voting:

The top 4 nominated by the community will move onto Final Voting which will happen from December 8 - December 14

 Joni Awards Ceremony:

On December 16, the community will all come together and join us in the #Atlas Amphitheater for an epic award ceremony!

### SantiMod
12/8/2022, 4:14:41 PM

@everyone  Community Alert  

While we cannot verify that Solana seed phrases created through Sollet.io or imported from Sollet to other wallets have been compromised, we urge everyone to remain safe by: 
- Using a hardware wallet (Ledger)
- Creating a new wallet and seed phrase in a different safe wallet
- Transferring your assets to the new wallet.

@everyone

Land Sale and Claim Stake Sales Happening Tomorrow!

It's almost time for the grand opening of the Sales for Land and Claim Stakes! 

Claim Stakes sales will commence 
CSS Land sales will commence 


 Land:

There will be 6 different tiers of land ranging from Base Tier to Tier 5. This is the first time that we'll be offering land and with that, comes awesome bonuses: 

• Inventory will be released in tranches with a discount up to 15% off!
• Residential estate on Central Space Stations (Beyond Tier 0) come with Cargo Storage and Landing pads
• Rewards for the original buyer: Ships, Crafting Stations, Pet Houses, Exclusive Ship Skins, Commemorative Badges, and more - depending on the Tier you purchase.
• Priority access to future land selection and commercial plot sales

  Claim Stakes:

There will be 5 different tiers of claim stakes ranging from Tier 1 to Tier 5. Claim Stakes will be activated in SAGE V1 to enable mining, crafting, starbase building and claim staking!

Before SAGE, Claim Stakes will have utility in Faction Fleet (SCORE) which will be resource production. The higher tier claim stake you own, the more resources it will produce.

Primary market buyers during the period December 20 - January 31 will receive an exclusive bonus airdrop of a Mining Drill and Power Plant, compatible with the acquired claim stake tier.

Read more about Claim Stake utility in SAGE: https://medium.com/star-atlas/cosmic-overture-begins-land-and-claim-stakes-up-for-grabs-in-phase-2-of-sage-start-sequence-f47fa9f2f6c3

 | https://play.staratlas.com/market/

### DominicVainMod
12/20/2022, 11:20:02 AM

@everyone

Claim Stake Sales Are Live!

Claim Stakes in Star Atlas are officially LIVE! Start building your galactic community, your empire, and have a place to call your own all within the endless universe of Star Atlas!

Claim Stakes are physical objects that must be transported to the desired planet, before claims can be made to any plot on its surface. Claiming these plots make infrastructure possible, by giving the owner access to the planet's unique resources. 

  HOLIDAY BONUS:

If you buy on the Primary Market between December 20 - January 31, you'll receive an exclusive airdrop of a Mining Drill and a Power Plant, both compatible with your selected Claim Stake tier!

NOTICE: ALL BONUS ITEMS WILL ONLY BE DELIVERED TO THE PURCHASING WALLET FROM THE PRIMARY MARKET

Claim Stakes purchased from any wallet that isn't the Star Atlas wallet on primary market will NOT receive the mining drill or power plant.

CSS Land purchased from any wallet that isn't the Star Atlas wallet on primary market will NOT receive the hab, ships, commemorative NFT, custom paint, plot selection white list, commercial land purchasing white list, and any other relevant perks associated with the sale.

All bonus items will be distributed in a period following the close of the sale on January 31, 2023.

CSS LAND WILL GO LIVE AT 3 PM EST

 | https://play.staratlas.com/market/?category=structure&itemClass=stake

@everyone

Land Sales Are Now Live!

The bravest and most adventurous space explorers can finally purchase plots of land on each Faction's Central Space Station (CSS)!

The Land available makes up to 10% of the total residential area of each Faction CSS, divided into 6 different tiers: from Base tier to tier 5 Land plots.

These tiers range from a single apartment, with just enough space for all the necessities, up to what can only be described as a galactic palace!

 Land Sale Perks:

•  ALL tiers come with: Hab, crafting stations, indoor/outdoor paint, ship skin, commemorative badge, and priority access to land selection and commercial plot sales
•  Tier 1 - Tier 5 come with: Ships
•  Tier 3 - Tier 5 come with: Pet Houses
•  Tier 4 and Tier 5 come with: Sculptures

  Land Sale Discounts:

All 6 tiers of Central Space Station land sales will be released in tranches, each with 2.5% of the total land being released at a time and with different discounts. 

•  First Wave: 15% off
•  Second Wave: 10% off
•  Third Wave: 5% off
•  Fourth Wave: 0% off

NOTICE: ALL BONUS ITEMS WILL ONLY BE DELIVERED TO THE PURCHASING WALLET FROM THE PRIMARY MARKET

Claim Stakes purchased from any wallet that isn't the Star Atlas wallet on primary market will NOT receive the mining drill or power plant.

CSS Land purchased from any wallet that isn't the Star Atlas wallet on primary market will NOT receive the hab, ships, commemorative NFT, custom paint, plot selection white list, commercial land purchasing white list, and any other relevant perks associated with the sale.

All bonus items will be distributed in a period following the close of the sale on January 31, 2023.

 | Learn more: https://play.staratlas.com/css-land-sale/

### DominicVainMod
1/9/2023, 2:57:03 PM

@everyone

Staff Impersonations

   There's been an increase in Employee and Mod impersonations lately. Please remember:

• Employees and Mods will NEVER DM YOU FIRST
• These impersonators will use our exact bio, profile picture and in some cases even Discord ID with invisible characters. 
• Please be skeptical of EVERY DM you receive.

 Some other important reminders:

• Never give out your seed phrase / private key to anyone. No one should ever need it for any reason.
• Any giveaways/promotions will be announced on official channels, never through direct messages.

Start Sequence Reward Distribution Update

Hey Everyone, we appreciate the patience you guys have all shown in regards to the Start Sequence rewards. 

We ran into an issue with gumdrop (the distribution contract), as we found it hasn't been maintained through Solana protocol upgrades. The team had to work on fixing that before being able to execute the drop. This is now fixed.

We're now working on: Staging all of the assets. The metadata storage, the marketplace listings, and then the actual drop.

These drops will happen as soon as the above mentioned are complete.

 Star Atlas x Jupiter Partnership Announcement

In response to the partnership, our CEO and co-founder Michael Wagner said, "This is a win-win for both communities and for the developers. We can't wait to see the impact it will have on the Star Atlas community and its Galactic Marketplace experience."

### DominicVainMod
3/10/2023, 9:37:22 PM

@everyone 

Important Galactic Marketplace Update

Two important notes.  First, we want to emphasize that ATMTA, Inc. did not have any accounts at Silvergate or Silicon Valley Bank, and does not have any material exposure to USDC.  Operationally, ATMTA is unaffected by these recent developments, but we want to express our sympathy for all those who have been affected.

Second, out of an abundance of caution due to significant volatility in the price of USDC, in about ten minutes, we will be removing our NFT sales that were denominated in USDC on the Galactic Marketplace.  Given the peer-to-peer nature of the Galactic Marketplace, on which orders are placed directly on the blockchain, we are unable to cancel or modify users’ existing orders.  Although we believe Circle’s USDC to be a critical and well-run backbone of the web3 space, we nonetheless urge all users of the Galactic Marketplace to exercise caution and consider the risks of maintaining any orders in USDC.  Please note that ATLAS-denominated orders on the Galactic Marketplace are unaffected by these developments.  We will reactivate USDC-denominated markets if and when appropriate and may explore activating other token denominations on the Galactic Marketplace.

We hope that everyone stays safe in these turbulent times.

We will provide additional updates as we have them.

### DominicVainMod
3/13/2023, 8:42:01 PM

@everyone

As you may know, earlier today select CSS Land & ships were listed on the Galactic Marketplace at extremely low prices.  This was an inadvertent error in the listing process that we have taken steps to correct.

We caught the error internally shortly after the incorrect listings went live.  We immediately disabled the further trading of affected, already-purchased assets.

Although our investigation (conducted with the assistance of Kudelski Security) is still underway, it appears that a formatting error in a listing script caused prices above 1000 USDC to become truncated.  Our internal quality controls did not catch this error before deployment because it was tested on an asset priced at less than 1000 USDC.  This error is limited to the listing script for primary sales and does not affect other aspects of the Galactic Marketplace, which otherwise is functioning normally.

Tomorrow, we will re-enable all disabled markets and re-list assets at the correct prices.  Once we have completed our investigation, we will provide another update if any further steps are necessary.

All other aspects of the Galactic Marketplace, SCORE, the DAO, and other Star Atlas services remain fully operational and unaffected by this isolated error.

Moving forward, we will continue working with our internal task force to ensure this does not happen again.  Thank you to our incredible team that caught the anomaly in almost real-time and sprinted to rectify it.  And as always, thank you to our ever supportive community.

---

### SantiMod
3/31/2023, 9:08:15 AM
_Edited_

@everyone

Star Atlas Q1 2023 Econ Quarterly Report Out Now!

 Our latest Economic Quarterly Report covers the foundations necessary for analyzing the Star Atlas metaverse business cycles, an essential aspect in understanding the state of our economy. 

The Economic Quarterly series represents a progressive research strategy aiming to establish the core tenets of our metaverse economics. The study of empirical and theoretical macro applied to the metaverse shapes the zeitgeist.

 The creation of economic data is crucial for the advancement and adoption of ideas. Therefore, we: 

• Defined a panel dataset equivalent to the country panel data sets frequiently maintained by OECD Statistics, International Monetary Fund, and Bank for International Settlements

• Applied the methods of McCracken and Ng (2015) to extract a domestic and global factor index. The dynamics factor approach is advanced in business cycle research and thus provides a natural starting point for summarizing the Star Atlas economy.

• Revisited the standard definition laid out by Burns and Mitchell (1946) to measure and define business cycle turning points.

• Compared the volatility of Bitcoin to U.S. GDP enabled us to justify a reduction in the minimum phase length assumption from 180 to 9 days. This parameter allowed us to identify turning points using the popular rule-based approach pioneered by Bry and Boschan (1971) and amended by Harding and Pagan (2002). Identifying recessions and expansions further ingrains the idea that metaverse economies are real economies. 

We hope you enjoy our State of the Economy series, a must-read for anyone interested in understanding the development of the Star Atlas metaverse.

 | To read our latest report: http://staratlas.com/newsroom/economic-reports?utm_medium=community

### SW4GN3R [STAR]
4/11/2023, 3:58:58 PM

Hello all,

I'm aware there is a lot of discussion surrounding Pablo's departure.  I can confirm he is no longer with the company, which was effective as of March 31.  I would like to keep the reasons for his departure private and wish him all the best going forward.

The transition after he left was straightforward and natural: I have been taking a more direct role in leading our revenue department, which includes marketing and growth strategies.  There haven't been any interruptions in our day-to-day operations, and I am focused on empowering a culture of excellence and creativity in the department and beyond.

I maintain total confidence in the path ahead for Star Atlas, and I am genuinely excited to share what we've been working on with you all.

### DominicVainMod
4/12/2023, 2:15:16 PM

@everyone

Faction Claims!

You can now enlist your Claim Stakes in Faction Claims!

Claim Stakes are the foundation of planetary gameplay loops in Star Atlas. They are physical objects that claim planetary plots, grant the owner access to extracting available resources, and build in-planet infrastructure.

 Enlisting your Claim Stake in Faction Claims will reward you with 4 vital resources for your intergalactic journey:
• Food
• Fuel
• Ammunition 
• Toolkits

 To enlist your Claim, follow these steps:
• Go to play.staratlas.com
• Connect your wallet
• Head to Faction Claims
• Enlist your Claim
• Accumulate resources over time

Don’t have a Claim Stake yet? We have you covered: https://play.staratlas.com/market/?category=structure&itemClass=stake&utm_medium=community

This is just the first use case of many that our space travelers will have. Keep an eye out for SAGE news, where your Claim Stakes will be even more critical to your galactic conquest.

For additional information, go to
https://staratlasgame.medium.com/star-atlas-faction-claims-space-mining-claim-stakes-feature-37e3b456da97

 | Enlist here: https://play.staratlas.com/claims/?utm_medium=community

### DominicVainMod
4/26/2023, 11:01:39 AM
_Edited_

@everyone

Star Atlas Build is Live! (IP Policy)

Star Atlas Build, the program that supports community-built projects and creators, is live!

Star Atlas is largely community-driven and built. We're excited to introduce the guidelines for commercial use of Star Atlas IP, so you can build an entire business on Star Atlas - with the first $1M USD being royalty-free!

Some Star Atlas intellectual property that will be available are:
• Faction logos & fonts  
• Ship, character, and location art  
• Story & lore information  
• A special "Star Atlas: Powered by the People" logo  

Assets that will NOT be included are:
• Source code  
• UE5 and WebGL animations and wireframes  
• WIP or drafts  
• The core Star Atlas trademarks  

Interested in creating a Star Atlas product or service? Fill out this form: https://share.hsforms.com/1fEP3-upUS92k3wwBFBdAEgc75gu

Learn more: https://medium.com/star-atlas/supporting-community-entrepreneurs-build-with-star-atlas-intellectual-property-first-1m-in-4753ecf31e35

We created a category of channels just for those interested in discussion around building. 
• ⁠🏁┃get-started 
• ⁠unknown 
• ⁠💻┃community-developers

 | Build: https://build.staratlas.com/?utm_medium=community

@everyone

⪛⦿⫺ Announcing Never Alone ⪛⦿⫺

Never Alone is a social campaign for this year, where you can find Star Atlas loot by collecting the Punaab Saand's lost memories!

Your objective in Never Alone is to help Saand recover the secrets of his past after losing his memories in a fateful ship crash. On your Never Alone journey, there will be 4 missions, each representing an arc of Saand’s past. The first mission, Scraps and Spoils, is live NOW!

Zealy  :
You'll complete your mission on Zealy, where you'll earn XP by fulfilling quests and use it to acquire Saand's Memories!
 Memory Glimpse (5,000 XP)
 Memory Fragment (6,250 XP)
 Memory Revelation (7,500 XP)

Zealy link: https://zealy.io/c/staratlas-never-alone/

Loot :
After each mission, redeem your Memories for mission loot, or save 3 of a specific Memory type until the end of the year and burn them for:

 Glimpses of a Forgotten Life
 Fragments of a Forgotten Life 
 Revelations of a Forgotten Life! 
All Memories will be available for trading on the Galactic Marketplace!

Check out the infographic below for exclusive mission loot, end-of-year loot and DAC loot information!

The choice is yours! By saving your Memories until the end of the year, you can also join a competition with your DAC! Combine points with your DAC members for fantastic in-game assets! More details to come on the DAC competition later this year.

Plus :
Keep a close eye on our social channels for more information, time-limited quests, and updates! In the meantime, learn more about the structure of Never Alone and the DAC competition: https://medium.com/star-atlas/never-alone-a-shared-social-adventure-across-the-star-atlas-galaxy-89cd90627234

 | Good luck on your Never Alone journey: https://staratlas.com/campaigns/never-alone?utm_medium=community

### DominicVainMod
6/1/2023, 11:41:30 PM

@everyone 

Star Atlas Showroom Release 2.1 is Out NOW On the Epic Games Store!

From wild racing tracks of the Volant Station to jetpacks, ALL ships being flyable, and much more, this closed-access release is the newest iteration of our Star Atlas playable metaverse! Let's go over the updates you can expect:

Ground Racing :
Challenge your skills in a time-trail contest vying for the global leaderboard, or relax and master the mechanics of racing! It's solo for now, but you can look forward to competing against other racers in the R2.2!

 All 49 Ships Flyable :
You heard that right. ALL 49 ships in the Galactic Marketplace are now flyable. Some are still in their greybox phase but you can now experience your ship(s) in different ways even if they're not full complete yet! Among the 49 flyable ships, there are 6 that now nearly complete (Opal Jet, Fimbul Lowbie, Fimbul Airbike, Pearce X6, Fimbul ECOS Unibomba, and Floydliner) as well as the Pearce X4 reaching Gold standard (fully complete!)

Experimental Mode :
Delve deeper into the Star Atlas development process with Experimental Mode! Once toggled in the main menu, this mode provides an inside look into WORK IN PROGRESS and UNFINISHED levels, and even gives sneak-peeks of unreleased characters.

Photography Career :
With R2.1 comes a new way to show off your elegant Star Atlas photos! Snap your shots, upload them to #photography from inside the game, and have a chance to receive your photo minted by us to your wallet through themed contests!

Test Fly Ships You Don't Own :
To make sure you find yourself the perfect ship, you will now be able to test fly ships from all manufacturers in our new Testflight feature! Ships will cycle every 3 days, starting today, June 1st, with Pearce and VZUS. Only Large sized ships and below are part of Testflight.

Galactic Marketplace Integration :
You can now buy and sell Star Atlas ships directly in-game!

Updated Dogfighting Arena 
Environment Updates  
Jetpacks 

Learn how to gain a closed-access key for EGS: ⁠No Access 

 | Watch the Showroom R2.1 trailer now: https://youtu.be/uFE0YPo-iHk

### DominicVainMod

@everyone

ATLAS Pairs Return to Galactic Marketplace at 20% Discount With a Celebratory 80% Discount On a Titan Ship!

We are once again listing ships in the Galactic Marketplace for primary sales in ATLAS - with an added 20% discount on these sales. Ships had been previously available for sale in ATLAS, but were temporarily made unavailable in late 2022.

With this move, much more of the total ship inventory supply is once again available, ready to fuel the growing Star Atlas economy and satisfy the demand for upcoming game feature releases, including the browser-based SAGE gaming loop and the updated Unreal Engine 5 game client.

All returning ship assets will have their initial prices in ATLAS based on a rolling seven-day average of the token’s price in USDC (in the final 7 days of May 2023), and prices will be readjusted periodically.

The entire lineup of assets made available anew on the ATLAS pair with a 20% discount represents 50 percent of all remaining available inventory, with the other half being available on the USDC pair at full price. The 20% discount on the ATLAS pair will remain in effect until further notice.

Individual assets listed under both ATLAS and USDC pairs will have the same pricing step structure as before, adjusted for the remaining available primary sale supply.

To celebrate the relisting of ATLAS pairings, we'll also be instituting a 80% discount on a Fimbul ECOS Superphoenix for a limited time!

Head to the Galactic Marketplace in the newly released Showroom R2.1 or on the web now to see the assets on offer in ATLAS. → https://play.staratlas.com/market & https://store.epicgames.com/en-US/p/star-atlas-bead34

 | Learn more: https://medium.com/star-atlas/atlas-spaceships-galactic-marketplace-big-discount-169210b9815e

### DominicVainMod
6/7/2023, 7:10:41 PM

@everyone

R4 Transition Announcement

Star Atlas is taking the first step toward a player-driven economy!

That first step is to conclude the sale of R4 from the Star Atlas DAO. We are also taking a few measures to bolster other R4 productive parts of the economy that help accommodate a smooth transition.

The Star Atlas DAO has been selling an infinite supply of Food, Fuel, Ammunition, and Toolkits (Also known as R4) since the release of Faction Fleet.  That infinite supply is being reduced to a one-time 30-day supply to transition to the players owning the R4 economy.

 Measure 1 - Claim Stake R4 Emission Increase:
With Claim Stakes, players will now receive massively amplified R4 production by enlisting them in Faction Claims!
Enlist Claim Stakes here: https://play.staratlas.com/claims/

 Measure 2 - Claim Stake listing for sale in ATLAS pairs:
Half of the remaining Claim Stakes primary sale is now AVAILABLE in the Galactic Marketplace in ATLAS, for 20% off!
Purchase Claim Stakes here: https://play.staratlas.com/market/?category=structure&itemClass=stake

 Measure 3 - SAGE: Escape Velocity R4 Emission Increase:
By scanning in Escape Velocity, R4 resource amounts will get a near-800% increase so that players can replenish their in-game resources!
Test Escape Velocity here: https://sage.staratlas.com/

Claim Stakes are the first asset to receive DIRECT economic utility in our ecosystem! Through this transitional period, they’ll maintain the R4 resource generation functionality and will have their intended purpose evolve together with the game.

All of these measures are subject to change during this process

To learn more about The Dawn of the Player-Driven Star Atlas Economy, check out the Medium article below! 

 | https://medium.com/star-atlas/claim-stakes-atlas-gameplay-star-atlas-economy-cf43e684b965

R2.1.1 Patch Update Now Live!

Our first patch for Showroom R2.1 is LIVE! Read on to learn more about what's in this new patch.  

PATCH NOTES:

GENERAL• Fixed an issue where players would launch the game for the first time and hadn't chosen a character, loading any game mode and ending up half underground in the hangar. 
• Added Ship Selection Screen to the Main Menu.
• Ship Selection and Player Selection screen is now active in loadout.
• Background Music is now persistent throughout all game modes.
• Fixed an issue where ESC to pull up menu and interact wasn't persistent across all screens.
• Fixed an issue where jetpack camera shake would persist after entering a ship.
• Added the ability for clients (non host) to see their projectiles when shooting.
• Fixed "Use Session ID" button.
• Updated West Outdoor Pad teleport location to prevent character being placed in the ground 
PHOTO MODE• Fixed an issue where the wrong photo was published in the Discord forum.
• Fixed an issue where exiting photo mode would cause a player to lose control of their ship. 
• Fixed an issue where "Gallery" wasn't loading photos taken.
• Fixed a bug where the 'R' key wouldn't enable rotation mode.
• Fixed an issue where photomode filters wouldn't work for client
GROUND RACING• Fixed an issue where some gates were not counted when passed near the border.
• Race can now be started by any player with the correct ship and not just the host.
• Fixed an issue where players could fly away from the racetrack after passing a few gates. Ground race track should support only hover mode now.
• Fixed the UI of the loading screen.
DOGFIGHTING ARENA• Fixed an issue where the NPC ships wouldn't give a player the chance to mount a ship.
• Fixed an issue where ships would blast off into the air when pressing F11 (Respawn).
• Fixed an issue where enemies weren't shooting the player
OUTPOST 39 (EXPERIMENTAL MODE)• Fixed an issue where the map would load too long during a Multiplayer session, resulting in players timing out. We extended the timeout period so the Flower Hunt game mode could be started.
SHIPS• Performance improvements.
• Animation fixes for the Opal Jet, Fimbul ECOS Unibomba, Pearce X4, Calico Medtech and Floyd Line Aerospace One.
• Fixed camera issues for a variety of ships.
• Fixed an issue where the Floyd Line Aerospace One lasers wouldn't show when firing.
• Fixed Floyd Line Aerospace One issue where client would see the pink landing gear Skeletal Mesh
• Fixed an issue where characters wouldn't disappear when mounting work in progress ships (Jetjet head).
• Adjusted sound mixing on several ships.
• Reduced interaction volumes on ships with interiors to prevent possessing the ship from outside the cockpit.
• Fixed an issue where the VZUS Opod wasn't flyable.
• Updated glass material to avoid flicker in 1st person camera mode for several ships.
CHARACTERS• Fixed an issue where some players would not be able to sprint after using the jetpack.
VOLANT AIR TRACK• Fixed several Volant air track targets that were far from their intended location
 | Play or wishlist now: https://store.epicgames.com/en-US/p/star-atlas-bead34

### SantiMod
6/28/2023, 9:03:11 AM

@everyone  SAGE: Escape Velocity Update - Loot Drop Refinement & Gameplay Conclusion
 
This announcement is for everyone playing SAGE: Escape Velocity and awaiting the next loot airdrop.

Sunsetting of SAGE: Escape velocity is on July 7, 2023.,Loot Distribution Date: EV loot will be released on Thursday, June 29th,Anti-botting measures are in effect: EV loot cap and bot identification,

Sunsetting of Escape Velocity Gameplay

SAGE: Escape Velocity (EV) was released in April 2023 as a technical showcase of revolutionary, real-time on-chain mechanics on Solana.

As a stress test at scale to enhance the robustness and resilience of all future releases of Star Atlas: Golden Era (SAGE), it has had an invaluable contribution to further game development.

As a sandbox test environment, we moved quickly with launching and updating EV, such as by introducing frequent updates, changes in mechanics, and additional features.  We wanted to make it as easy as possible for players to jump in and start participating in true on-chain gaming—and we have seen significant success on this front with player engagement levels increasing dramatically and with the team able to gather valuable information on player behavior.

With enough information gathered and lessons learned for future use, the primary purpose of EV is now nearing completion, which means a conclusion to this massively popular feature test. We will therefore be sunsetting Escape Velocity on July 7, 2023.

For players who want to continue gathering R4 resources themselves, you will be able to do so through the use of Claim Stakes and soon-to-be released Mining Ships in the Faction Claims app (https://play.staratlas.com/claims).
 
For those playing Never Alone, please make sure to finish all Escape Velocity-related quests before the closure date.

Introduction of an EV anti-botting loot cap & loot distribution

In both the wind-down period of EV and in the future, we are looking to further improve on the experience for players based on the data gathered during the test. One category of insight that we are acting upon immediately is botting. We have identified a small percentage of participating wallets that have made unauthorized use of automation software (“bots”). Although there are only a handful of addresses engaged in botting, they account for a significant amount of total rewards scanned in EV to date.

As the unauthorized use of automation software diminishes the player experience as well as goes against the Terms of Service, we are introducing a ceiling, effective retroactively, on the amount of loot botting addresses are eligible to receive in the upcoming EV loot airdrop on June 29. The ceiling was set based on an analysis of player participants in EV, and does not exceed the amount that a genuine human player could have obtained. Botting addresses will not receive any discovered higher-tier rewards (Gold, Platinum, or Diamond) and will receive a capped amount of lower-tier loot (i.e., R4).

Instead, lower-tier loot discovered by botting accounts in excess of the ceiling will be distributed to all human EV participants at a rate proportional to their own discovery of loot from June 15 onward. This EV loot will be released on Thursday, June 29th.

Furthermore, now on until its closure, any EV player whose activity is determined to be that of automated services will not receive any of the loot discovered.

Going forward, we may take more aggressive actions against wallet addresses that engage in botting activity, including by eliminating any loot scanned by a botting address. We hope that these actions and the increasing complexity of SAGE over time will slow the proliferation of botting activity. We appreciate the reports we have received on suspicious bot activity; your comments and feedback are, as always, very welcome.

Power to the People!

@everyone

Introducing Star Atlas DAO Proposals!

It's time to make YOUR voice heard!  

Introducing Star Atlas DAO Proposals, the first step to creating the most decentralized, player-owned economy. By you, for you!

With the introduction of DAO Proposals, you'll be able to view, comment, and vote on the very first POLIS Improvement Proposal (PIP-1)!

PIP-1 contains 3 articles to define all present and future Star Atlas DAO operations:
 Blockchain Supremacy Clause, defining our DAO as autonomous programs that operate on Solana
 Star Atlas Constitution, explaining all that the governance framework pertains
 Star Atlas Foundation, ratifying the operations of the Star Atlas DAO

Our roadmap for PIP-1 includes 4 phases:
 Declaration or the publication of PIP-1
 Deliberation, featuring public comments, debate and ongoing community interest voting
 Decision, the on-chain vote
 Democratic Convergence, the formal blockchain ratification of PIP-1

PIP-1 is an invitation to all who have locked POLIS in the POLIS Locker and received PVP, or POLIS Voting Power. PVP is going to be needed to participate in the proposal process. Lock POLIS here: https://govern.staratlas.com/lockers

To learn more about the Star Atlas DAO & how it works: 
https://staratlasgame.medium.com/star-atlas-dao-foundation-pip-sustainable-governance-in-gaming-39105cc0121f

PLEASE NOTE: While the Star Atlas DAO is live, we are still optimizing its performance for the high user volume. There may be possible outages upon the launch while we're improving the resilience of the infrastructure. If you experience timeout while accessing the DAO website, please refresh the page.

 SAGE: Escape Velocity Update  

The day has arrived. SAGE: Escape Velocity has come to an end.

As announced at the release of Destination Starbase in June, we have sunset SAGE: Escape Velocity.

Thanks to the entire community for turning it into a massively popular feature test, and you're an invaluable contribution to further game development by testing and sharing feedback on this revolutionary real-time on-chain game feature. It will be reflected in the increased robustness and resilience of all future releases of Star Atlas: Golden Era (SAGE).

You will still be able to fly around the map at sage.staratlas.com, however, the loot scanning function will no longer be available.

Loot
Final distribution of Escape Velocity loot will take place next week. It will include loot discovered from June 30 through the end of EV. Bonus loot that was confiscated from bots last week will also be part of this loot drop. 

Again, if you want to continue gathering R4 resources yourself, you are able to it through Claim Stakes and Mining Ships in the Faction Claims app.

@everyone

Introducing: Photography Career Contest!

Grab your photography drone, capture the beautiful world of Star Atlas, and have a chance to sell your winning photo on the Galactic Marketplace!  

How it works:
A theme will be announced and participants will have 4 weeks to showcase their photography skills. A panel of internal judges and the community will select one image a week for 4 weeks. At the end of the 4 weeks, the four winning images will compete against each other, and will be voted on again to find the winner!

The winning photo will be minted to the photographer responsible and we'll provide Galactic Marketplace support to sell their winning photo on as posters! Once a winner is chosen, a new theme will be announced, and the process will repeat.

How to participate:
Launch Star Atlas on the Epic Games Store,Use "Photo Mode" to capture a photo,Press Esc -> Extra -> Photo Gallery,Select the image you wish to publish, and it will be shared in ⁠📷┃photography  for the community to see and vote on (Note: you can publish one photo per day),
════════════════

The Photography Career Contest starts today and the first theme is... Ships!  

 | More information on voting, criteria, and timelines: https://medium.com/star-atlas/shoot-for-the-stars-star-atlas-launches-metaverse-photography-career-contest-bf1a5146fdee

### SantiMod
7/19/2023, 2:39:41 PM

@everyone 

Star Atlas CORE is Back!

After a short break, we're excited to welcome you back into Star Atlas CORE with the release of Act 2 - Episode 1! 

In this Episode, a survivor seeks justice for the carnage left in the wake of our three explorers. Are Gyun, Moda, and Timpo brave - or insane - enough to continue their journey? Can Timpo’s time vortex device pave the way to safety, or will our adventurers soon realize what it’s like to have their minds fold into oblivion?

### SantiMod
7/24/2023, 10:08:49 AM

@everyone  Today ATMTA is announcing a major change in its operation. Michael Wagner, the CEO and co-founder of Star Atlas, has addressed the changes in a detailed letter to you, and will host an update to the community in the Atlas Amphitheater on Wednesday, July 26, at 1:00pm Eastern Time.
Here is the summary of everything that is happening:

ATMTA is restructuring its team, making a hard decision to say goodbye to many passionate and talented builders of Star Atlas.,The restructured team will focus on delivering SAGE and the newly announced Crew Mobile App.,The CORE graphic novel will continue to be released, with the DAC platform being nearly ready for launch.,Development of the Unreal Engine 5 game will resume at a significantly slower pace while still producing future releases. The same goes for the DAO governance system.,This strategic move enables uninterrupted development, ensuring stability for the runway to launch multiple products.,The strategic refocusing also makes Star Atlas more attractive to capital partners with shared values.,
The full letter is attached at the end of this message. 

Got questions? Please ask them in ⁠unknown and join us for answers in the update to the community with Michael Wagner in ⁠🎤┃Atlas Amphitheater on Wednesday, July 26, at 1:00pm Eastern Time.

  What is the Atlas Brew?
The Atlas Brew is a weekly community gathering, where we discuss your favorite Star Atlas topics and have fun! We take notes during the Atlas Brew and give them to the team, so your voice matters!

### DominicVainMod
8/11/2023, 8:39:27 PM

@everyone

Patch Notes - Ship Config (V2)

We just implemented our patch to ship configs. Read on to learn more about the highlights of the patch. 

PATCH NOTES:• Implemented various fixes to ensure consistent adherence to V2 rule sets outlined in the Star Atlas Lore Wiki
• Adjusted Crew, Components, and Mods across all ships to ensure consistent ordering
• Updated ship dimensions to match latest work done in Unreal Engine 5
• Gave the Pearce F4 and Pearce X4 a Cargo module to be more consistent with their description. Implemented other minor module tweaks
• Adjusted Calico Guardian, VZUS Ballad, Pearce T1, and the Fimbul BYOS Tankship weapons. Adjusted some slower ships to be given turrets in lieu of fixed weapons
• Adjusted Bombers to be more consistent in their bomb bay packages, but have reduced fixed weapons
• Added Utility Rigs to several ships that were missing them
• Added Janitors and other crew members that were missing from several ships
• Made minor adjustments to the Opal Jet, Opal Jetjet, Fimbul Mamba and Pearce X5 descriptions
• Adjusted Drone ports across all ships to be correct total class and quantity
• Added stealth to the MFG bonus table for VZUS
• Adjusted the VZUS opod and VZUS ambwe to no longer sport undersized heat sinks

 NEW: Fimbul Mamba Ex (Will Never be Sold)Intimidation is a lot cheaper than ammunition.

When they rebuilt the Mamba into the Mamba Ex, Fimbul's goal was to remind your enemies that things might go better for them if they just raise their hands, instead of their weapons.
Calico Maxhog (Will Never be Sold)Built literally to get away from... everything we could think of.

The Maxhog marks Calico's sporty, aggressive entry into the proper civilian transport market. With its all-terain capabilities, it can drive, fly, and go underwater!

@everyone

Ship Configuration V3

Exciting news! An update to our ships with Ship Configuration V3 is coming and you'll be able to feel these changes first in SAGE Labs!

Your feedback on Ship Configuration V2 has been heard, and we're making direct adjustments assisted by your input. These adjustments include:

 Ship descriptions now properly match their configuration
 Components are no longer counterproductive to manufacturer bonuses
 We're dropping Component Upgrades for select ships to bring them back in line with their origination price

Stat updates aren't reflected on https://play.staratlas.com/, they'll be reflected after the launch of SAGE Labs.

Also, as a reminder, ship configurations are ever-evolving. Stay tuned for future adjustments to crew and interior modules!

 | Learn more about Ship Configuration V3: https://medium.com/star-atlas/star-atlas-3rd-generation-ship-configuration-system-9c067d2e681

### DominicVainMod
10/4/2023, 3:18:06 PM
_Edited_

@everyone

SAGE Labs Developer Tools and Documentation

 Star Atlas is opening doors to development for Solana builders and creators!  

Use open-platform Star Atlas developer tools to securely build a live economy, linked to real life, a unique possibility in the blockchain industry. The toolset also makes it possible to play the whole game via an Application Programming Interface (API), enabling anyone to build their own entire front end and functionality for the game.

It includes all the tools we use to connect to the blockchain and everything needed to build interactions on the blockchain.

Other examples:
  Data source: A core helper library for all our Solana interactions
  Player Profile: Fully usable
  Atlas Prime: Can be implemented on any app

Learn more: https://medium.com/star-atlas/star-atlas-opens-free-development-solana-builders-creators-sage-labs-programs-1d6cbcdd33d7

If you have any questions or want to collaborate with others, check out the ⁠💻┃community-developers channel!

 | Use our tools and documentation: https://build.staratlas.com/

Attachments:
- F7jHhp9acAA6biQ.png — https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/799478132993425429/1159222941087715338/F7jHhp9acAA6biQ.png?ex=6a57eafe&is=6a56997e&hm=ac00d315bb1f02299916a8410bb5ab8d52dd9a48622ab3e60b28ef16fc639900&

@everyone

Foundation Room is Changing

Hey everyone, we're adjusting the Foundation Room starting today to be gated. Our most committed community members will have access to our dev team to ask questions and see early sneak peeks into our development!  

There's going to be three ways to gain access to the Foundation Rooms:
• Verify that you have 80,000 PVP (Polis Voting Power) which can be obtained by locking your POLIS at https://govern.staratlas.com/
• Reach level 45 in our Discord server
• Complete Never Alone quests and collect memory fragments

In the Foundation Rooms, you'll have access to:
• Foundation Room - A room dedicated to asking questions and giving feedback directly to our team
• Foundation Room Chat - Chat with other Foundation Room members
• Foundation Room Sneak Peeks - Raw and early sneak peeks into our development that you can't find anywhere else

We look forward to seeing you there!

 | Verify here:  https://matrica.io/home
 | Find a step-by-step guide here: ⁠✍┃fr-verify

### DominicVainMod
12/13/2023, 11:14:29 AM

@everyone

Big Marketplace Change

 Attention Star Atlas community  

A big and exciting change is coming to the Galactic Marketplace.  

We will be removing the USDC pairings on Resources and Skins making the ATLAS pairing the sole means of trading these assets. 

ATLAS becoming the sole pairing on select Galactic Marketplace items is a pivotal step in the evolution of the Star Atlas economy.

Note: We've also repriced ATLAS pairings on all primary asset sales

 | https://play.staratlas.com/market/

Everything Update

There's a lot happening right now and we don't want to bombard your notifications, so we're going to add all the updates into this one announcement! Read on for an economics pre-announcement, Starcomm update, and marketplace update.  

  ECONOMICS PRE-ANNOUNCEMENT
Like mentioned before, we're making an effort to pre-announce economic changes vaguely so everyone isn't completely caught off guard by our patches. With that being said, the economics team has big changes coming to SAGE Labs and Faction Fleet (SCORE) that will happen within the next 2 days.

We'll provide details of this update when it's live.

 STARCOMM UPDATE
We're aware many of you faced issues with Starcomm today, and we get how frustrating that can be. Good news: after collaborating with our RPC data stream provider, we identified and have a resolution coming for today's issue.

 GALACTIC MARKETPLACE UPDATE
Tonight we'll be launching the seasonal sale of Armstrong IMPs (111 quantity in USDC and 111 quantity in ATLAS at 25% off), along with an ATLAS repricing to bring those prices inline with the recent volatility.

This seasonal sale will last until January 8.

### SW4GN3R [STAR]
12/22/2023, 12:08:04 AM

@everyone 

We are aware of issues some users are experiencing related to pending ATLAS earnings in Faction Fleet following the reward rate adjustment earlier today. 

Prior to executing that reduction, we ran a settlement process on our end to lock in pending reward values. However, given network congestion on Solana recently, a number of those settlement transactions failed.,
We will be reverting the earnings reduction back to the previous rate, which will concurrently adjust previous pending rewards to their original amount,
Following that adjustment, we will again downward adjust the earnings rate in Faction Fleet,
For now, DO NOT claim your rewards,
We also have logs of user claims executed within this window and will be able to provide the appropriate ATLAS rewards if they were less than the appropriate amount,
Give us the day tomorrow to sort through this. After that time, please contact support if you feel you were impacted and uncorrected. We will resolve this before studio closure.

### DominicVainMod

@everyone

Star Atlas State of the Economy - Q4 2023

The latest Star Atlas State of the Economy report for Q4 2023 is out! 

A major theme this quarter was navigating the economic shifts brought by the introduction of SAGE Labs. The addition of new gameplay loops brings in fresh economic opportunities.

Key Highlights Include:
Daily SCORE participation shifted above the mean trend for the first time since the start of its decline in 2021.,The ONI and USTUR factions waited for strong ATLAS/USDC price action to re-enter SCORE, while the MUD faction consistently  re-entered over time.,Aggregate census wealth grew by 302%.,SAGE Labs supported 1,550 daily active wallets on average throughout the quarter.,Surpluses of Golden Tickets produced by USTUR and ONI found a market in the MUD faction, leading to a substantial wealth exchange.,Food, fuel, ammunition, toolkits, and survey data units showed incredible strength in their USDC valuation throughout the quarter.,
Read the full detailed report  

 | https://staratlas.com/newsroom/economic-reports

@everyone

Surge Technical Test - Starting Soon

Get ready to help us test the new faction vs. faction vs. faction game mode, Surge, in 15 minutes!    

How to play Surge
Press "Play" in the Main Menu,A "Surge" play card will appear at 11AM PT / 2PM ET, click that,Select a faction to represent,Eliminate opposing faction players to gain "tags" (note: If you die while holding tags, the player who eliminated you will gain your tags),Players with at least 10 tags are marked as high value,Bring earned tags to marked extraction locations to secure points for your faction,The faction with the most points at the end wins!,
Known list of bugs: ⁠📢┃minor-announcements⁠

If you have feedback or experience bugs not present in the above list, please use ⁠No Access. See you there!

@everyone

Thank you for Helping us Test!

Hey everyone!

Firstly, we want to extend a huge thank you for your invaluable participation in our multiplayer technical test and for testing Surge! Your feedback has been immensely valuable to us. 

Undoubtedly, there were performance issues and bugs present, that's why we decided to conduct several Discord-only tests before we promote a public one with economic incentives. 

We extensively tested Surge beforehand but there are some issues that only surface when we really put things to the test with hundreds of players. This is part of the development process and we assure you, things will only get better from here. 

Your patience and understanding means a lot to us, and we're going to be sharing a post mortem next week to outline our findings and lessons learned.

@everyone

SAGE Labs Starbased Update

Next week, alongside the deprecation of the old build of SAGE Labs and the implementation of new SDU scanning dynamics we will be implementing two additional changes to SAGE Labs Starbased:

Reduction in Starbase upkeeping requirements,Adjustment to how ATLAS is distributed at the end of each epoch. There will now be 4 tiers for ATLAS emissions within each faction. A faction must contribute a minimum amount of LP in order to progress to the next tier. For example, Tier 1 will emit (x) ATLAS while Tier 2 emits 2(x). Each tier will have a specific total faction LP contribution needed in order to unlock that tier of ATLAS emissions. (Numbers to be announced),
These changes are expected to take place mid-to-late next week, stay tuned!

### DominicVainMod
4/17/2024, 1:41:28 PM
_Edited_

@everyone

Surge Rewards

The Surge test on April 20 features four tiers of rewards that are based off how many players join the test, those are:

 > 300 players = ATLAS 
 300+ players = Common Crew
 500+ players = Uncommon Crew
 1,000+ players = Rare Crew

At each tier of crew rewards, only one faction will be distributed to all participants in the test regardless of faction, determined by the faction with the highest number of wins up to that tier. For example, if Ustur has the most wins before reaching 1,000 players, only the Rare Crew associated with Ustur will be minted for every tester regardless of faction. This logic applies to the Common and Uncommon Crew as well.

Make sure you mark interested on the Surge events at the top left of the Discord to make sure you don't miss it!

@everyone

Starbased Changes 

Hey everyone, thank you so much for all the feedback you've been giving on Starbased. We understand there's some uneasiness spread throughout the community while you've been waiting to hear about adjustments. We get it, which is why we're here today to announce changes that we were planning to announce later, closer to release.  

Changes coming in the next 24-48 hours:
Increase the total daily ATLAS emissions to 6 million ATLAS (from 4.5 million ATLAS),Increase the LP reward for supplying SDUs to 1,100 from 450,Starbase upgrades will now persist into the future. (Note: While they will persist now, we can and will still change the map in terms of size and number of starbases as we see appropriate,Crafting fee update,
Changes coming in a few days to couple weeks:
ATLAS emissions will now scale with Starbase upgrades within a faction. Each Starbase upgrade will increase faction daily ATLAS emissions. Full release details will be public when this change goes live,Changes to upkeep. When Upkeep levels of food are high [low] crafting speeds are faster [slower] and upkeep burn rates are faster [slower].,Adding a game resource export tax. There will now be a fee to export goods from the game which will make hopping factions more difficult. More details closer to release. Note: This change is only intended to hit those constantly hopping factions, not the everyday player (This can come in the form of 2 options: 1. Wait for local markets to implement this change or 2. Have the option of paying a tax or going through a waiting period of (x) hours.),
We look forward to hearing your feedback on the changes outlined and thank you for your patience during this time. 

The team will be talking in the Atlas Brew about these changes right NOW in ⁠🎤┃Atlas Amphitheater

Recording of the Atlas Brew, where @Chri.z and @Deleted User discussed these changes: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B9fYOle3UQs

Mentions: @Chri.z, @Deleted User

### DominicVainMod
7/26/2024, 2:28:40 PM

@everyone

Star Atlas Airdrop - Coming August 9

The largest airdrop in Star Atlas history is coming August 9! It's simple. For every ship you own on the snapshot date (August 8), you get an airdrop.  

What will be included in this airdrop?
Crew will be airdropped as Crew Packs, and ship components will be airdropped as "Ship Component Bundles". Currently, ships on our marketplace come with crew and components. After this airdrop, these will need to be acquired separately.

Crew airdrop logic
For every crew member your ship came with, you'll receive a crew pack containing one character. The rarity of your ship determines the tier of the packs you get:
 Common/Uncommon Ship - Silver Packs
 Rare/Epic Ship - Gold Packs
 Legendary/Anomaly Ship - Platinum Packs

 | For more details on the airdrop, crew packs, and the snapshot date, read this article: https://medium.com/star-atlas/crew-packs-and-star-atlas-airdrops-are-coming-in-august-important-dates-utility-in-sage-labs-a261baa7a3b6

### DominicVainMod
8/20/2024, 7:01:06 PM

@everyone

Crew Cards - Addressing Feedback and Making Changes for the Health of the Game

Hey everyone! Firstly, thank you for all the support you've shown for Crew Packs. We appreciate every comment, and it’s amazing to see you all having fun. We've been listening to your feedback, taking notes from our team, and heavily considering the overall health of the game. As a result, we’re making some important changes to Crew Packs and your Crew Cards. Let's get into it!  

New Traits  
Some of you shared your passionate feedback on the MUD species, so we're adjusting accordingly and also adding some new outfits to other species! • New MUD hairstyles have been added.
• MUD now have increased chances to roll an augment or trinket trait.
• MUD have decreased chances to roll a helmet trait.
• New outfits have been added to MUD, Mierese, Punaabs and Sogmians that offer a wider variety of patterns and colors.
New Algorithm and New "Episode"  
The rate at which higher-tier traits were rolled on lower-tier rarities and lower-tier traits were rolled on higher-tier rarities was way out of our comfort zone. Simply put, it made all the card rarities look the same. You noticed it, and we did too. We’re not exaggerating when we say that years of work from one of the best character art teams in gaming went into creating a cohesive visual language. Our goal was to ensure that each card's rarity is immediately recognizable, with distinct silhouettes, color grading, and storytelling elements to enhance immersion. Since we didn’t hit that mark, we’re making adjustments. We’re rolling out a new algorithm for Crew Pack openings that will significantly reduce the chances of cards rolling "out of rarity" traits. In other words, Commons will look truly Common, and Legendary crew will genuinely look Legendary. Along with this algorithm change, we're also moving from "Episode 0" cards to "Episode 1".
• Art on previously opened cards will reroll using our new algorithm at the time of this announcement to Episode 1 art. Your old art will still be viewable as Episode 0 art. 
• Episode 1 cards will keep Rarity, Species, Sex, Aptitudes and Name. Only the art and traits are adjusting. 
• Anomaly art will be retained, you should see very little difference between your Episode 0 and Episode 1 art.
• Episode 0 won't be UE5 compatible. The latest episode art will be used at the time of adding UE5 support. 
• Added a drop down menu to "My Crew Cards" that lets you select alternate art.
• Anna Tolle, Sammy Banx and the Surge Crew will remain unchanged.
• In the episode 0 algorithm, aptitudes had an even chance to roll. We're changing this and now certain aptitudes will be more rare than others. The good news is that we're not changing your already rolled aptitudes for Episode 1. If you rolled a rare aptitude you get to keep it. Consider it an early bonus of opening packs!
What's Next for Crew Packs?  
Now that we've gotten through all of today's changes, what's next?• Crew backstories.
• Share feature.
• Adding full res PFP downloads in layers, full body or headshot.
• Adjusting Punaab eyes.
• Updated Ustur cloak.
• Adding the "background" of your cards to the "My Crew Cards" viewer.
• Adding SAGE crew to the "My Crew Cards" viewer.
Known Bugs to be Fixed:  
The amount of Crew Cards listed on the "My Cred Cards" tab may not match the amount in your wallet. This will be fixed tomorrow.,You may see black boxes instead of the new art, this should fix over time leading up until tomorrow.,The drop down menu to view previous episodes isn't implemented yet.,
Now that these changes are live, we're live on Tensor! However, the artwork might take a bit to update on their site. To ensure everything is fully updated, we recommend holding off on trading until tomorrow. We'll share the link and announce when it's ready.
