@everyone

Dawn of the Freighter - SAGE Labs Update Coming Tomorrow

Tomorrow marks a major leap forward for the SAGE Labs economy with the introduction of Local Markets and the return of RFRs (under a new name)!

Local Markets  
Trade resources with other players in Galia's individual sectors through local markets, mini economies within the larger SAGE Labs economy! It's time to build your strategy and dominate these localized trading hubs!

The Return of RFRs Under a New Name  
RFRs are making a comeback with a new name: MUD, USTUR and ONI Infrastructure Contracts! Craft these contracts and keep an eye on the newly introduced local markets to see which sectors need resources. ATMTA will place buy orders in three sectors at a time, per faction, rotating periodically. 

More details about the release will be given when the update goes live tomorrow. There won't be a set release time, keep an eye out for an announcement!

What's New?

A heartfelt thank you to all of you for your incredible support throughout 2024. We wouldn’t be here without each and every one of you. If you haven’t already, be sure to check out our latest update on the Epic Games Store!

Happy Holidays, and we’ll see you in 2025!

### SW4GN3R [STAR]
1/9/2025, 10:22:16 PM

Hi @everyone,

In light of recent growing frustrations with the performance of SAGE Labs onchain mechanics, I wanted to take a moment to address here publicly some recurring community questions about any concerns we have as a team about the long term viability of "fully onchain gaming," as well as communicate some of the possible solutions we are, and have been, considering. I'll preface by emphasizing that there is no silver bullet, and that every potential solution comes with trade-offs. There is also no immediate solution we can implement. However, we have experienced these spikes in user activity on Solana in the past during periods of high volatility, and they tend to subside when things stabilize for a while, leading to better game performance and lower fees. But as we've seen Solana grow in popularity, there is no reason to expect we won't face similar issues going forward.

So, for full clarity, I'm going to be focusing this post on two issues:
 Transaction Settlement Reliability: do the actions you take in game settle onchain? (on the first attempt!),Transaction Fee Impact: how much do you have to pay in SOL to play? (can users play profitably?),
In responding to these questions, I need to talk a little bit about why we're even building game logic onchain in the first place, as well as the core ethos/philosophy of ATMTA in building Star Atlas. The entire concept of Star Atlas centers on this idea of a globally accessible, open, permissionless, and decentralized open world space adventure MMO (and metaverse integration). That's a whole lot of crypto buzzwords, but it's something I feel deeply passionate about (as does the team). If we're truly going to accomplish building a cybernation with a self sustaining, global and borderless economy, managed by a new political system and set of rules (the DAO), Star Atlas needs to be censorship resistant. It can't just run on ATMTA servers in the long run. And while it is going to take tremendous effort to accomplish that goal, building game logic via smart contracts (onchain programs) is arguably the first step towards decentralization of the Star Atlas universe.

There are other benefits to building onchain, such as composability and extensibility. This simply means that other developers, whether that be organized teams or individual contributors, can build out applications that integrate with Star Atlas seamlessly. Which is why we created https://build.staratlas.com/, to help facilitate this co-creation of Star Atlas. And we've seen a number of incredible applications come from it: SLY Tools, ATOM (up-and-coming), EveEye, Aephia dashboards, many others, and many more to come. And this extends to entrepreneurs leveraging the open Intellectual Property policy, enabling non-ATMTA companies to form and monetize products using Star Atlas IP (e.g. Galia Merchants). And finally, onchain logic in many ways makes our backend systems more secure and reliable. I'll post a little excerpt here from Jacob, our co-founder and CTO, about some of these benefits:

It's hard to fully express how awesome it is from an engineering & security perspective having the fully on-chain game systems.  Many MMO projects struggle for years to solve problems that are solved for us by default by building fully on-chain, particularly related to data security & authorizing user actions.

-Jacob Floyd

In a nutshell, that's the "why" we're building our architecture the way that we are. And we have no intentions of changing that. We set out to build a world-changing MMO, and this blockchain integration is an integral part of that vision.

Which leads to the question of, what are we going to do to improve the user experience. Fortunately, this topic is something we have been considering for the better part of a year. Though it hasn't really been a pressing or prioritized challenge to solve until more recently. And we do intend to future proof Star Atlas.

---

### SW4GN3R [STAR]
1/9/2025, 10:22:33 PM
_Author inferred from message grouping_

I'd also like to note here that the team has been working tirelessly on infrastructure improvements to ensure that transaction issues aren't related to Star Atlas specifically. There's still room to improve, but dramatic improvements have been made, and many more are in the process of being implemented (Starcomm v2, StarFrame, IronForge, etc.). Setting that aside for the moment, we need to solve for exogenous variables outside of our control (i.e. network congestion and priority fees).

There are several potential avenues ahead of us, including:
 Apollo (likely rebranding) / AtlasNet -- ATMTA's Solana clone/fork, which we've been leveraging for internal program testing,SVM/L2 solutionsMagicBlock,Sonic,,Moving to a new layer 1,Game logic changes to reduce transactions,
I'm going to come back to Apollo. So, starting off with some of the SVM alternatives, I'll note there are some interesting products out there. And there very well could be a short term implementation of one or several of these solutions. However, the downsides consist of additional reliance on third party solutions, as well as a general lack of true decentralization. Referring back to my comments about our core philosophy, it's imperative to us that Star Atlas can operate long into the future, without the requirement for ATMTA to provide and maintain the infrastructure (years away). 

Considering a new blockchain protocol, particularly for SAGE, lacks any real viability. Given the considerable number of programs we have already deployed, and inconsistencies or incompatibility with base language, data structures, and general code logic would imply a complete re-write of every one of the programs we've created for SAGE. Years of work. And realistically, we would be moving away from the blockchain that has already captured significant mindshare and market share, alongside the interest of countless developers that can be targeted to build applications supporting the Star Atlas ecosystem. Solana is also a network that has arguably been the most stress tested and battle hardened. Any other network achieving comparable levels of success would likely succumb to the same pitfalls, and challenges for our players, that Solana is presenting to us now. Sure, ATMTA could receive a substantial grant to transition, but it would set us back years. And again, we're still moving away from a clear winner.

I've seen a number of requests to make changes to game logic to reduce the number of transactions, similar to what we did with SDU mechanics. On this, all I can say is that I'm strongly opposed to making changes to game design simply because we have a short term technology limitation or challenge. Gameplay is the cornerstone of Star Atlas. If we make the game terrible just to reduce costs, we're never going to succeed. That's not to say that we won't make changes to game design over time, but I certainly do not want those decisions to be a result of protocol choice. The game needs to be fun, and needs to match what game design wants to see. Period.

Which finally leads us to Apollo. And to be honest, we weren't prepared to fully reveal any details about it. Dan is currently working on the addendum I referenced during the year-end Town Hall, and details are soon to be released. Apollo in it's most basic form, as it presently exists, is already functional. It's a fully centralized layer 1 purpose-built for Star Atlas testing. Meaning it already runs the exact same programs that we deploy on Solana mainnet, just in a private version of Solana for us. The future of Apollo could very well be a fully decentralized network, synchronous with Solana, optimized for Star Atlas. We have a significant opportunity in front of us given we already have a decentralized organization generating cash flows from gameplay -- the Star Atlas DAO. Meaning we have an avenue to compensate validators on Apollo.

---

### SW4GN3R [STAR]
1/9/2025, 10:22:48 PM
_Edited_
_Author inferred from message grouping_

Again, I don't want to get in to specific roadmap details for Apollo in this post. And to be clear, a move in this direction would also mean years of work. But some of the potential benefits could include:
 Zero-fee network transactions for users,Initially, zero network congestion, with the DAO given authority to permit new games/projects/programs later,A network optimized for Star Atlas,Validators compensated via the DAO (perhaps the first form of revenue distribution),POLIS locking requirements for validators,Licensing/Node sales to validators,State hashes secured on Solana, further hardening Apollo security and retaining the relationship with Solana,Solana programs easily re-deployed on Apollo,
To be clear, Apollo would not be an L2 rollup solution. It would be an independent, fully decentralized network, over time. But it would leverage one of the most performant blockchain protocol codebases in existence today, and be potentially security hardened by Solana's network state. 

This is the absolute TLDR version of what Apollo could become. More from us in the near future. But I wanted to reassure everyone that we are thinking about these issues. We do want a positive gaming experience for everyone in Star Atlas today, and all of the future players/creators/builders/entrepreneurs we see joining. And at the risk of sounding repetitive, you all are participating in the bleeding edge of innovation. Which means we're going to hit some bumps in the road. But we're going to overcome any obstacle in our way, and we're going to make this thing a reality.

Power to the People.

---

We're continuously looking to improve how our tokens integrate with the game, and the ATLAS Locker is up next to get some exciting enhancements: 
 7 tiers (changed from 5).

 Reduced Fleet Respawn timer - Higher tiers unlock larger reduced timers.
 Exclusive NPC Merchants - Access special deals.
 Locker Specific Recipes - Unlock locker specific assets like more efficient resource recipes and cosmetics.
 SAGE AI Assistant - Get access to SAGE, an AI assistant made to help you manage fleets, mining, crafting and more future game features.
 Blockchain Fee Subsidies (DAO approval required) - Higher tiers receive higher subsidies.
 Lower Resource Consumption in Faction Fleet (Near to mid-term benefit only) - Optimize your Faction Fleet efficiency while it's still around!
 ATLAS Locker Skill Tree - Unlock progression for various market-related activities and use points to specialize your style via a skill tree.
 Fleet Rental Fee Discount - Higher tiers unlock larger discounts.
 Fleet Rentals Token Earnings Share - Using the liquidity locked into this feature, unsold primary ship inventory will be rented out, with earnings distributed to locker participants based on their ATLAS locked.

### DominicVainMod
3/31/2025, 2:56:09 PM

@everyone

Star Atlas Quarterly Economic Report - Q1 2025

The latest Star Atlas Quarterly Economic Report is LIVE!  

HIGHLIGHTS:
The ONI faction earned 12% more ATLAS this quarter than MUD and USTUR,,dethroning MUD as the most productive despite the large wealth disparity.
The Golden Carnival created approximately 158 million ATLAS worth of resource burn,this quarter, while simultaneously stimulating the economy through ship prize drops.
Star Atlas GDP contracted by 44% this quarter amid volatile markets, but showed,signs of recovery toward the end of the period with the release of the Fleet Rental
program.
The fleet rental program generated over 1 million ATLAS per day for lenders,,supported by an 80% contract acceptance rate across factions.
Active fleets grew by 15% on average post fleet rental release, and ship classes such,as small and x-small saw considerable increases in demand.
Local market volume share surpassed 30% excluding transactions occurring at the,CSS. Large discrepancies in price between markets provided opportunity for
arbitrage.

 | Download and view the full report: https://staratlas.com/newsroom/economic-reports

Attachments:
- Star_Atlas_Q1_2025_-_Wide.png — https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/799478132993425429/1356356416948146246/Star_Atlas_Q1_2025_-_Wide.png?ex=6a57e5d9&is=6a569459&hm=1bd1e6490f9ec4461f73c80814ba9e2740c3a829d68cac0a671c9eb7f4a9748b&

Join The Vantarah and Help Test Star Atlas

Star Atlas is searching for a select group of elite testers to become the pioneers among pioneers. Introducing The Vantarah, an officially recognized group by ATMTA, dedicated to testing the earliest builds and features of Star Atlas UE5.

While this is a volunteer position, members will receive special benefits, including a unique Discord role and icon as well as asset rewards. If you are passionate about Star Atlas, want to help make it the best game possible, and have the time to test, this is the role for you.

How we are selecting The Vantarah members:
Priority will be given to those who are active within the Discord community.,Priority will be given to those who have the time required to test effectively.,
Important note: This will be the only time we open registration for this role. After the initial group of testers is selected through the Google Form, all future testers will be handpicked by the team based on Discord activity.

Registration closes on

### DominicVainMod
6/11/2025, 4:38:36 PM

SAGE Labs Transition to C4 Update

Hey everyone, we're increasing the stakes for our future C4 update!

If your faction has upgraded a Starbase to Tier 5 in SAGE Labs, your faction will automatically control all core systems within that Starbase’s region when C4 launches. However, If your Starbase is below Tier 5 before the C4 launch, your faction will need to capture core systems to gain control of that region.

So get out there, rally your faction, and secure your dominance before launch!

### DominicVainMod
6/30/2025, 3:44:54 PM

@everyone

Star Atlas Quarterly Economic Report - Q2 2025

A new Star Atlas Quarterly Economic Report is LIVE!  

HIGHLIGHTS:
Despite the 41% increase in daily ATLAS emissions this quarter, the swap volume of,emitted ATLAS remained at only 5% of decentralized exchange ATLAS volume on
average.
For the first time in Star Atlas history, employed groups such as citizens and residents,now control over 70% of the total wealth within the ecosystem.
The ATLAS token locker reached a new all-time high locked balance of 2.147 billion,ATLAS.
Fleets rented from the Star Atlas Fleet Rental Program account for 10% of all active,fleets within SAGE Starbased.
The XS ship class saw 12% appreciation this quarter as one of the most dominant,ship classes used in rental fleet compositions.

 | Download and view the full report: https://staratlas.com/newsroom/economic-reports

### DominicVainMod
8/27/2025, 3:59:24 PM

Town Hall Important Announcements/Recap,Thank you all so much for joining us today for the last Town Hall of Star Atlas Summer! If you weren't able to join, we have you covered.

NEW PATCH + EXCLUSIVE RESOURECE IN UE5  
We’re introducing Ink, a brand-new exclusive resource tied to XP earnings in our UE5 game. For the first time, you’ll be able to earn inside our immersive experience!

Alongside Ink, this update also brings weapon balance changes, a fix for hard wallet authentication issues, and more. Full patch notes will drop with the release coming later this week.

To celebrate, we’re running a Double XP Weekend from August 29–31 meaning... DOUBLE THE INK EARNINGS!  

Few important notes on Ink:
XP Conversion: 100 XP = 1 Ink,Distribution: Ink won’t appear instantly in your wallet. It will be airdropped periodically to help us manage distribution and prevent bad actors.,Utility: Ink can be used in SAGE Labs. You’ll be able to deposit it into Phantom Starbases as an upgrading resource, valued at 100,000 LP per Ink. This connects our experiences like never before.,
 SAGE LABS: NEW PHANTOM STARBASES  
We’re introducing "Phantom Starbases" to SAGE Labs, designed to serve as an infinite sink. These bases will always remain at Tier 1 and will never progress to Tier 2.

Phantom Starbases are ephemeral, meaning they won’t carry over into C4. However, all materials normally required to upgrade a starbase from Tier 1 through Tier 5 can still be deposited into them.

SAGE EDITOR SUITE (C4 DEVELOPMENT TOOLS EDITOR)  
We've just released an interactive tool for the Star Atlas Community that gives a look behind the curtain of C4 with development tools that we, the ATMTA team, use ourselves.

 | https://ses.staratlas.com/

OPEN SOURCING STAR FRAME  
We're proud to give back to Solana by open-sourcing Star Frame!

Star Frame is a new framework built on Pinocchio to help developers builds complex, secure, and scalable programs, unlock even more innovation on Solana. 

 | Learn more: https://medium.com/star-atlas/open-sourcing-star-frame-building-the-next-generation-of-solana-programs-87fa9b375338

MISSED THE TOWN HALL? WATCH THE RECORDING HERE: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=AKvbmSHZNgo

@everyone

### DominicVainMod
10/1/2025, 1:43:53 PM

@everyone

Star Atlas Quarterly Economic Report - Q3 2025,A new Star Atlas Quarterly Economic Report is LIVE!  

HIGHLIGHTS:
Daily ATLAS emissions dropped by an average of 10.5%, with simultaneous record high,volatility observed throughout the quarter.
The citizen group increased its wealth to new heights, owning over a quarter of,aggregate wealth within the Star Atlas ecosystem
The Star Atlas GDP contracted this quarter by 26%, primarily due to token volatility,Earnings per dollar across wealth groups showed that high wealth accounts between,1k-10k outperformed the whale and medium wealth groups. 
Holosim captured a unique subset of active players, negligibly impacting the,Starbased active user base. 

 | Download and view the full report: https://experience.staratlas.com/newsroom/economic-reports

Iris' Blessing Has Arrived: Double XP Weekends and $5,000 in Monthly Prizes,Iris' Blessing calls out to citizens all over Galia. Riches, luck and fun are in everyone's future and you're not going to want to miss it. For the next six months, enjoy monthly double XP weekends and drawings worth over $30,000!  

MONTHLY DOUBLE XP WEEKENDS   
First Double XP Weekend: October 24 - October 26

Back by popular demand, we're bringing back double XP weekends! Mark your calendars for the below 6 weekends where you'll be able to earn DOUBLE the Ink. Play in official gunplay and racing matches, and for every 100 XP, earn 1 Ink! Soon, double XP weekends in Star Atlas will directly contribute to the z.ink airdrop, allowing you to earn twice the XP, twice the Ink, and twice the z.ink rewards.

MONTHLY DRAWINGS  
First Monthly Drawing: November 14

Every second Friday of the month, you'll have a chance to turn in tickets earned from joining Discord community events! Whether it's an Atlas Brew, an Economic Forum, or a Game Night, collect your ticket and submit it through our Discord bot for a chance to win your share of the monthly drawing! Keep an eye out for exclusive challenges and activities that will give out tickets as well!

Claim your first code for 100 tickets using 'Iris Blessing'.

Make sure you check in everyday by typing !gm! The more often you check in, the more tickets you'll get. 

 | Learn about dates, prizes and instructions: https://medium.com/star-atlas/iris-blessing-has-arrived-double-xp-weekends-and-5-000-in-monthly-prizes-a84375dfaa5c

### DominicVainMod
12/18/2025, 3:35:25 PM

Galactic Marketplace Changes + New Ship + Claim Stake Earn zXP Now!,Hey everyone, making a joint announcement to let you all know the latest and greatest! 

#1 NEW SHIP PRICING MODEL IS LIVE  
ATMTA will now act as an active market participant, listing ships closer to true player demand.

For already introduced assets, we'll be listing ships closer to secondary prices. It's important to add that we'll only be adding our listings to ships with current demand. 

New ship listings will be priced using live data from comparable assets, reflecting real market conditions. This brings healthier pricing, better discovery, and a more realistic marketplace.

Here are the assets with new listings:
Armstrong IMP,Fimbul ECOS Unibomba,Calico Medtech,Rainbow Arc,Ogrika Ruch,Ogrika Sunpaa,Pearce R6,Fimbul Lowbie,Fimbul BYOS Tankship,Pearce MR8,Claim Stakes (Tier 1 - Tier5),
#2 PEARCE MR8 RELEASE  
To mark the launch of the new pricing model, the highly anticipated Pearce MR8 has just hit the Galactic Marketplace.

A large, multi role powerhouse built to handle everything Galia throws at you. 

 | Get it here: https://play.staratlas.com/market/PMR8pgX8mTwbYLDsxhQ1SMdVZzNttY3kca65TV7WqMg/?symbol=USDC

#3 CLAIM STAKES EARN ZXP NOW  
We’re continuing to expand the ways you earn zXP.

You can now enlist your Claim Stakes into Faction Claims and begin earning zXP. More actions. More progression. More reasons to participate.

@everyone

### ⪛⦿⫺ZeSKK [STAR]
1/27/2026, 1:03:17 PM

Starcomm Removal Update - LIVE NOW

Hey everyone! 

Today, we're introducing a significant overhaul to our backend infrastructure. We have replaced Starcomm (v2) with a direct-to-RPC solution. While this has been tested internally and stress tested in Holosim, we are requesting that you submit any bug reports to us should you identify any issues with data accuracy across the ecosystem. We're continuing to work on improvements for a new version of Starcomm (v3).

Here's what's changed:

Starcomm removed from Claim Stakes
Starcomm removed from Galactic Marketplace
Starcomm removed from Fleet Rentals
Starcomm removed from SAGE Labs

We've tested everything thoroughly and consider this ready for release. If you notice any issues with loading or data refreshing, please report them to the team so we can patch quickly.  

@everyone

---

### SW4GN3R [STAR]
1/30/2026, 3:38:16 PM
_Edited_

@everyone,

We are here to stay, but I have some difficult and important news to share today.

In response to the ongoing market conditions and the need to align our expenses more closely with current revenues, we've made the tough decision to restructure parts of the team. These steps are essential to extend our runway and keep pushing forward on the long-term vision of Star Atlas; something we've done in prior cycles to reach where we are now.

This round hits the community especially hard. With a heavy heart, I'm announcing that we've had to eliminate several key front-facing roles, including those held by @DominicVain and @⪛⦿⫺ZeSKK. These departures follow @Santi's recent decision to start his own venture (completely unrelated to this restructuring).

Dominic, Jose, and Santi have been among our most passionate voices, representing Star Atlas publicly every day with energy and dedication. Their contributions over the years have been immense, and words can't fully express my gratitude for their tireless efforts. These were not easy decisions; if the opportunity arises, I'd welcome them back in a heartbeat.

On a brighter note:Jose remains fully committed to our weekly community events, including Atlas Brew and Lorekeepers. (Also, keep an eye out for his upcoming PIP which he will be posting shortly).,We're also preparing a couple of new economics-focused events to roll out soon.,We have a number of team members who will continue contributing to the project for a time in an unpaid capacity.,
The team is now leaner, but intensely focused. We're pouring everything into delivering considerable updates for Holosim, C4, and z.ink in the coming weeks. A tremendous amount of work has already gone into these and I'm genuinely excited about their potential to reignite growth and bring more energy to the ecosystem. 

This journey has never been easy, and we never expected it to be. We're incredibly fortunate to still have some of the brightest talent in the industry driving Star Atlas forward.

So today we say farewell (for now) to friends, colleagues, and true dreamers. But the mission continues. There's significant potential for momentum building, and a lot to look forward to very soon.

Thank you for your continued support and belief in what we're building together.

-Michael

Mentions: @DominicVain, @⪛⦿⫺ZeSKK, @Santi

---

### Xcode [STAR]
3/10/2026, 1:18:57 PM

transmission begins

Captains—Holosim Chapter 2 is live .

bridge displays surge with new data as the navigation array locks onto uncharted sectors

Chapter 2 brings an entirely new layer of strategy, progression, and competition to the Expanse—and I've got the full briefing right here.

 A New Storyline & Tutorial,Every Captain has a story, and Chapter 2 brings yours to life. Three faction-specific storylines await—whether you serve under MUD, ONI, or USTUR, you'll follow a unique narrative with characters and missions tailored to your allegiance. It's the best way to experience what Star Atlas is all about, and newcomers will find the revamped tutorial gets you from recruit to operational faster than ever.

Oh, and Captains who see their storyline through to the end? You'll earn an exclusive cosmetic reward. Consider it a medal for your service.

 Territory Control,This is where things get strategic. Factions now compete for sector control across the galaxy, tracked through Dominion Points visible right on your bridge displays. Every sector claimed, every starbase defended—it all feeds into your faction's dominance over the Expanse.


 Mining Achievements,Hundreds of sector-based mining achievements are now scattered across the galaxy, each tied to specific resources and territories. Completing them awards Global Rank XP that climbs you up the leaderboard, plus Zink XP to fuel your progression.


 The Marketplace,The galactic marketplace has been seeded with NPC orders, so you'll find active buy and sell opportunities from day one. We've also calibrated asteroid richness values across the sectors to ensure a balanced economy. Supply chains are ready—time to turn those raw minerals into profit, Captain.

 Notification System,I've been upgraded . Your ship's AI now runs a full notification system keeping you informed in real time. Mining operations complete? You'll know. Achievement milestone hit? Logged and delivered. Enemy fleet entering your sector? You'll get the alert before they're in weapons range.

No more flying blind out there. I've got your back on mining status, achievement progress, combat warnings, and more—all routed straight to your bridge.

 Battle Log & Combat UI,Combat just got a serious overhaul. The brand new battle log gives you a complete record of every engagement—who attacked, what they brought, and how it played out. Combined with the redesigned combat UI, you'll have full tactical clarity during and after every fight.

No more wondering what happened to that missing fleet. Every encounter is documented.

 Systems Upgrade,Behind the scenes, we've fully migrated to direct RPC data, retiring the old Starcomm v2 relay entirely. What does that mean for you? Faster, more reliable data across every system on your bridge—fleet status, marketplace prices, sector control, all of it. Smoother operations across the board.

---

sensor grid pulses as new Chapter 2 protocols finish loading

The Expanse just got bigger, deeper, and a whole lot more competitive. Whether you're here for the storyline, the territory wars, the leaderboard climb, or all of it—Chapter 2 is your proving ground.

Get out there, Captain. The galaxy is watching.

transmission ends

Sage AI - Fleet Operations Coordinator

@everyone

P.S. If you are already a Zink subscriber, make sure you use the in game banner to link your Holosim account. Do not start the process from the Zink dashboard. See here for details;  ⁠📢┃minor-announcements⁠

sensor grid recalibrates — corrected reward manifest incoming

 Prize Tiers — Corrected

#1 — 1× Pearce MR8,#2 — 1× Armstrong IMP Tap,#3 — 1× Ogrika Tursic,#4–10 — 1× Fimbul Mamba (replaces the Opal Bitboat),#11–30 — 1× Armstrong IMP Tip,#31–100 — 1× Busan Thrill of Life,#101–200 — 2× Explorer Pack,#201–258 — 1× Explorer Pack,More than 1,000,000 XP — 1× Explorer Pack,
 Inside every Explorer Pack: 1× Pearce X4 · 1× VZUS Solos · 1× Fimbul ECOS Unibomba · 1× Ogrika Ruch. A starter quartet to round out the hangar.

communication relay flags an updated action item

 Action Required — Link Your Mainnet Wallet (New Deadline)

Prizes route on-chain, which means we need a destination. Link a mainnet wallet to your Holosim account by Friday, May 8, 2026 at 11:59:59 PM UTC.

This is the final extension — the deadline has been pushed to give every eligible Captain a last opportunity to get their wallet on file. After the deadline, any accounts without a linked mainnet wallet, with eligible wallets shift up to fill the missing slots . Distribution will run Saturday, May 9th following curation.

No linked wallet by the deadline, no delivery vector — your prize will be redistributed to the next eligible Captain in line. — get that wallet connected.

transmission ends

### Jindo | Star Atlas Mod [STAR]
5/26/2026, 12:55:26 PM

NEW DISCORD SCAM ,SCAM AWARENESS
Our team has become aware of yet another new discord scam. This post is simply to let our community know. @everyone

How It Works
Random users will reply to you with a "Show More" at the bottom of their msg.,Clicking this links you to another discord (DISCORD WARNS YOU AT THIS POINT),The scammers will, "assist" you in the new discord server you have joined.,
The Star Atlas discord and z.INK discord will most likely not encounter this issue as we have proper security measures in place already. 

AS ALWAYS, STAY SAFE, DO NOT TAKE EXTERNAL LINKS FROM UNTRUSTED SOURCES 
All support for Star Atlas and Zink will be handled through our official channels. Always ask a Mod or Team member if you have questions.

Attachments:
- Screenshot_2026-05-26_124319.png — https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/799478132993425429/1508891327306137783/Screenshot_2026-05-26_124319.png?ex=6a57c98e&is=6a56780e&hm=8d29628875f7654c81a39473cd89011af62bdf1a8acf8da69804d4089554f255&

C4 PTR Release + New Promotional Sale + Crew Pack Snapshot! ,To celebrate the release of the C4 PTR, we are running a promotional sale featuring brand-new, highly anticipated Star Atlas assets.

The promotion will run for exactly 2 weeks or until the limited listings are depleted. 

We will run a snapshot of all those who purchased the assets during the campaign period and send them the bonus crew packs after the two weeks have passed.

#1 CULTIVATION CLAIMS (TIERS 1-5) 
Cultivation Claims represent the pinnacle of interspecies collaboration by CARY. State-of-the-art planetary structures designed to harness the galaxy's most elusive crops, resilient plants, and exotic herbs. By unlocking the unique properties of exotic flora, these installations transform barren worlds into high-yield agricultural hubs, ensuring that no matter how harsh the frontier, your people will thrive.

Here are the available tiers and their crew pack bonuses:
Tier 1: $15 // 1,337 units // 1x silver 1 crew pack,Tier 2: $75 // 400 units // 3x gold 1 crew pack,Tier 3: $274 // 128 units // 1x platinum 5 crew pack,Tier 4: $639 // 62 units // 2x platinum 5 crew pack + 1x gold 5 crew pack,Tier 5: $1,970 // 25 units // 6x platinum 5 crew pack,
 | Get it here: https://play.staratlas.com/market/CULTyJq7cqCyTxcReRffiGgv3XrKJCfBhYVVrkdNVgSV/?symbol=ATLAS

#2 VZUS ARMA RELEASE 
Born in the turbulent aftermath of the Convergence War, the Arma is a small fighter vessel commissioned by the Winter Fist Sect. Now fully integrated into the Ustur fleet, it serves as a stark reminder: while the Ustur seek enlightenment through peace, they are perfectly capable of finding truth in combat and destruction.

Pricing and bonuses:
VZUS Arma: $81 // 185 units // 3x gold 1 crew pack,
 | Get it here: https://play.staratlas.com/market/VZA31QjDrGs6rEXZs6JN2shsG6GbWZZst51qUHNvNnX/

#3 CALICO FLATTOP LAUNCH 
A behemoth of heavy logistics. This capital freighter utilizes a revolutionary magnetic pulse to secure cargo, ensuring flawless transit without disturbing even the frailest goods. Equipped with an atmospheric generation shield to protect hauls from deep-space radiation, it embodies Calico’s philosophy of strength through commerce.

Pricing and bonuses:
Calico Flattop: $3,050 // 20 units // 12x platinum 5 crew pack,
@everyone

 | Get it here: https://play.staratlas.com/market/CALHEsUGywdyXybMi3DAUgWCNZwxP55Wj2Ean8wXqho4/

### Jindo | Star Atlas Mod [STAR]
6/3/2026, 12:06:42 PM

Compromised Discord Account of EX Team Member,Chypto's Discord account has been compromised
Chypto is an EX team member with ATMTA,He has many friends in the community,His compromised account is sending everyone DMs with a link to a discord among other things.,Please BLOCK & REPORT this account if you have any interaction with it. (right click > block > send report),
DO NOT ENGAGE WITH THIS ACCOUNT OR ANYONE CLAIMING TO BE THIS PERSON
This account was removed from Star Atlas, Zink, and all internal services in months past and does not pose any immediate threat,This message is just a heads up to @everyone of our players that might have been friends with him or any players that received a DM from him,
Simple steps to stay safe and avoid these things
Always use 2FA on discord, your web browser login, or anywhere else that contains information you don't want someone to access,Avoid using browser password saves as much as possible,If a direct message seems off for one reason or another, it most likely is. INVESTIGATE,NEVER CLICK ANYTHING WITHOUT VERIFIYING ITS LEGITIMACY,

Attachments:
- image.png — https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/799478132993425429/1511778168694898889/image.png?ex=6a57be22&is=6a566ca2&hm=ed10bdecd5702cf9727f731ab33ebaf8e740edf04d57f2c03ea6ea2a0af36b02&

(right click > block > send report) , DO NOT ENGAGE WITH THIS ACCOUNT OR ANYONE CLAIMING TO BE THIS PERSON This account was removed from Star Atlas, Zink, and all internal services in months past and does not pose any immediate threat , This message is just a heads up to @everyone of our players that might have been friends with him or any players that received a DM from him , Simple steps to stay safe and avoid these things Always use 2FA on discord, your web browser login, or anywhere else that contains information you don't want someone to access , Avoid using browser password saves as much as possible , If a direct message seems off for one reason or another, it most likely is. INVESTIGATE , NEVER CLICK ANYTHING WITHOUT VERIFIYING ITS LEGITIMACY ,

### SW4GN3R [STAR]

Hello @everyone,

Today we are releasing a material (extraordinary measure) draft proposal to the DAO seeking reimbursement for historical expenses related to establishing the Star Atlas Foundation, service providers, and tax liabilities incurred related to DAO revenues. This is a big deal, so I wanted to make you all aware of the proposal, which can be found here: ⁠ATMTA Historic Expense Reimburs…

I will be joining the Brew next week to cover a special segment on this proposal. In the meantime, I look forward to your questions and feedback in the proposal thread itself. We will be covering financial specifics, rationale, and impact to the DAO Treasury.

I want to be clear that this request is not essential to survival presently, but the additional funding backstop will provide much greater confidence to deliver on all of the near term objectives surrounding SAGE C4, UE5, z.ink, and beyond, without further disruption to the team.

-Michael

Genuinely, thank you to everyone who continues supporting us through every challenging moment we've encountered. It means a lot.

-Michael
